01591| (defgroup denote-sort nil
01592|   "Sort Denote files based on a file name component."
01593|   :group 'denote
01594|   :link '(info-link "(denote) Top")
01595|   :link '(url-link :tag "Homepage" "https://protesilaos.com/emacs/denote"))
01596| 
01597| (defconst denote-sort-comparison-fallback-function #'string-collate-lessp
01598|   "String comparison function used by `denote-sort-files' subroutines.")
01599| 
01600| (defconst denote-sort-components '(title keywords signature identifier random last-modified)
01601|   "List of sorting keys applicable for `denote-sort-files' and related.")
01602| 
01603| (defcustom denote-sort-identifier-comparison-function denote-sort-comparison-fallback-function
01604|   "Function to sort the DATE/IDENTIFIER component in file names.
01605| The function accepts two arguments and must return a non-nil value if
01606| the first argument is smaller than the second one."
01607|   :type 'function
01608|   :package-version '(denote . "4.0.0")
01609|   :group 'denote-sort)
01610| 
01611| (defcustom denote-sort-title-comparison-function denote-sort-comparison-fallback-function
01612|   "Function to sort the TITLE component in file names.
01613| The function accepts two arguments and must return a non-nil value if
01614| the first argument is smaller than the second one."
01615|   :type 'function
01616|   :package-version '(denote . "3.1.0")
01617|   :group 'denote-sort)
01618| 
01619| (defcustom denote-sort-keywords-comparison-function denote-sort-comparison-fallback-function
01620|   "Function to sort the KEYWORDS component in file names.
01621| The function accepts two arguments and must return a non-nil value if
01622| the first argument is smaller than the second one."
01623|   :type 'function
01624|   :package-version '(denote . "3.1.0")
01625|   :group 'denote-sort)
01626| 
01627| (defcustom denote-sort-signature-comparison-function denote-sort-comparison-fallback-function
01628|   "Function to sort the SIGNATURE component in file names.
01629| The function accepts two arguments and must return a non-nil value if
01630| the first argument is smaller than the second one."
01631|   :type 'function
01632|   :package-version '(denote . "3.1.0")
01633|   :group 'denote-sort)
01634| 
01635| (defcustom denote-sort-dired-extra-prompts '(sort-by-component reverse-sort)
01636|   "Determine what `denote-sort-dired' prompts for beside a search query.
01637| This concerns the additional prompts issued by `denote-sort-dired' about
01638| whether to sort by a given file name component and to then reverse the
01639| sort.
01640| 
01641| The value is a list of symbols, which can include the symbols
01642| `sort-by-component', `reverse-sort', and `exclude-regexp'.  The order is
01643| significant, with the leftmost symbol coming first.
01644| 
01645| These symbols correspond to the following:
01646| 
01647| - A choice to select the file name component to sort by.
01648| - A yes or no prompt on whether to reverse the sorting.
01649| - A string (or regular expression) of files to be excluded from the results.
01650| 
01651| If the value is nil, skip all prompts.  In this scenario, the sorting is
01652| done according to `denote-sort-dired-default-sort-component' and
01653| `denote-sort-dired-default-reverse-sort'."
01654|   :type '(radio (const :tag "Do not prompt for anything" nil)
01655|                 (set :tag "Available prompts" :greedy t
01656|                      (const :tag "Sort by file name component" sort-by-component)
01657|                      (const :tag "Reverse the sort" reverse-sort)
01658|                      (const :tag "Exclude files matching regexp" exclude-regexp)))
01659|   :package-version '(denote . "4.0.0")
01660|   :group 'denote-sort)
01661| 
01662| (defcustom denote-sort-dired-default-sort-component 'identifier
01663|   "Set the default file name component to sort by.
01664| This is used only if `denote-sort-dired-extra-prompts' omits the
01665| minibuffer prompt for which file name component to sort by."
01666|   :type '(radio
01667|           (const :tag "Sort by identifier (default)" identifier)
01668|           (const :tag "Sort by title" title)
01669|           (const :tag "Sort by keywords" keywords)
01670|           (const :tag "Sort by signature" signature)
01671|           (const :tag "Random order" random)
01672|           (const :tag "Last modified" last-modified))
01673|   :package-version '(denote . "4.1.0")
01674|   :group 'denote-sort)
01675| 
01676| (defcustom denote-sort-dired-default-reverse-sort nil
01677|   "If non-nil, reverse the sorting order by default.
01678| This is used only if `denote-sort-dired-extra-prompts' omits the
01679| minibuffer prompt that asks for a reverse sort or not."
01680|   :type 'boolean
01681|   :package-version '(denote . "3.1.0")
01682|   :group 'denote-sort)
01683| 
01684| ;; NOTE 2023-12-04: We can have compound sorting algorithms such as
01685| ;; title+signature, but I want to keep this simple for the time being.
01686| ;; Let us first hear from users to understand if there is a real need
01687| ;; for such a feature.
01688| (defmacro denote-sort--define-lessp (component)
01689|   "Define function to sort by COMPONENT."
01690|   (let ((retrieve-fn (intern (format "denote-retrieve-filename-%s" component)))
01691|         (comparison-fn (intern (format "denote-sort-%s-comparison-function" component))))
01692|     `(defun ,(intern (format "denote-sort-%s-lessp" component)) (file1 file2)
01693|        ,(format
01694|          "Return smallest among FILE1, FILE2 based on their %s.
01695| The `%s' performs the comparison."
01696|          component comparison-fn)
01697|        (let* ((one (,retrieve-fn file1))
01698|               (two (,retrieve-fn file2))
01699|               (one-empty-p (or (null one) (string-empty-p one)))
01700|               (two-empty-p (or (null two) (string-empty-p two))))
01701|          (cond
01702|           (one-empty-p nil)
01703|           ((and (not one-empty-p) two-empty-p) one)
01704|           (t (funcall (or ,comparison-fn denote-sort-comparison-fallback-function) one two)))))))
01705| 
01706| ;; TODO 2023-12-04: Subject to the above NOTE, we can also sort by
01707| ;; directory and by file length.
01708| (denote-sort--define-lessp identifier)
01709| (denote-sort--define-lessp title)
01710| (denote-sort--define-lessp keywords)
01711| (denote-sort--define-lessp signature)
01712| 
01713| (defun denote-sort-random (elements)
01714|   "Shuffle ELEMENTS of list randomly."
01715|   (let* ((elements (copy-sequence elements))
01716|          (shuffled-list nil))
01717|     (while elements
01718|       (let* ((list-length (length elements))
01719|              (element (nth (random list-length) elements)))
01720|         (setq elements (delq element elements))
01721|         (push element shuffled-list)))
01722|     shuffled-list))
01723| 
01724| (defun denote-sort-modified-time-greaterp (file1 file2)
01725|   "Return non-nil if FILE1 modified time is greater than that of FILE2."
01726|   (let* ((attributes1 (file-attributes file1))
01727|          (mod-time1-raw (file-attribute-modification-time attributes1))
01728|          (mod-time1-seconds (time-to-seconds mod-time1-raw))
01729|          (attributes2 (file-attributes file2))
01730|          (mod-time2-raw (file-attribute-modification-time attributes2))
01731|          (mod-time2-seconds (time-to-seconds mod-time2-raw)))
01732|     ;; NOTE 2025-06-23: We normally sort using a "less" approach, but
01733|     ;; here we want to capture the semantics of "last modified"
01734|     ;; without relying on a reverse sort.
01735|     (> mod-time1-seconds mod-time2-seconds)))
01736| 
01737| ;;;###autoload
01738| (defun denote-sort-files (files component &optional reverse)
01739|   "Returned sorted list of Denote FILES.
01740| 
01741| With COMPONENT as a symbol among `denote-sort-components',
01742| sort files based on the corresponding file name component.
01743| 
01744| With COMPONENT as the symbol of a function, use it to perform the
01745| sorting.  In this case, the function is called with two arguments, as
01746| described by `sort'.
01747| 
01748| With COMPONENT as a nil value keep the original date-based
01749| sorting which relies on the identifier of each file name.
01750| 
01751| With optional REVERSE as a non-nil value, reverse the sort order."
01752|   (let ((files-to-sort (copy-sequence files)))
01753|     (if (eq component 'random)
01754|         (denote-sort-random files)
01755|       (let* ((sort-fn (pcase component
01756|                         ((pred functionp) component)
01757|                         ('identifier #'denote-sort-identifier-lessp)
01758|                         ('title #'denote-sort-title-lessp)
01759|                         ('keywords #'denote-sort-keywords-lessp)
01760|                         ('signature #'denote-sort-signature-lessp)
01761|                         ('last-modified #'denote-sort-modified-time-greaterp)))
01762|              (sorted-files (if sort-fn
01763|                                (sort files sort-fn)
01764|                              files-to-sort)))
01765|         (if reverse
01766|             (reverse sorted-files)
01767|           sorted-files)))))
01768| 
01769| (defun denote-sort-get-directory-files (files-matching-regexp sort-by-component &optional reverse omit-current exclude-regexp)
01770|   "Return sorted list of files in variable `denote-directory'.
01771| 
01772| With FILES-MATCHING-REGEXP as a string limit files to those
01773| matching the given regular expression.
01774| 
01775| With SORT-BY-COMPONENT as a symbol among `denote-sort-components',
01776| pass it to `denote-sort-files' to sort by the corresponding file
01777| name component.
01778| 
01779| With optional REVERSE as a non-nil value, reverse the sort order.
01780| 
01781| With optional OMIT-CURRENT, do not include the current file in
01782| the list.
01783| 
01784| With optional EXCLUDE-REGEXP exclude the files that match the given
01785| regular expression.  This is done after FILES-MATCHING-REGEXP and
01786| OMIT-CURRENT have been applied."
01787|   (denote-sort-files
01788|    (denote-directory-files files-matching-regexp omit-current nil exclude-regexp)
01789|    sort-by-component
01790|    reverse))
01791| 
01792| (defun denote-sort-get-links (files-matching-regexp sort-by-component current-file-type id-only &optional reverse exclude-regexp)
01793|   "Return sorted typographic list of links for FILES-MATCHING-REGEXP.
01794| 
01795| With FILES-MATCHING-REGEXP as a string, match files stored in the
01796| variable `denote-directory'.
01797| 
01798| With SORT-BY-COMPONENT as a symbol among `denote-sort-components',
01799| sort FILES-MATCHING-REGEXP by the given Denote file name
01800| component.  If SORT-BY-COMPONENT is nil or an unknown non-nil
01801| value, default to the identifier-based sorting.
01802| 
01803| With CURRENT-FILE-TYPE as a symbol among those specified in
01804| the variable `denote-file-type' (or the `car' of each element in
01805| `denote-file-types'), format the link accordingly.  With a nil or
01806| unknown non-nil value, default to the Org notation.
01807| 
01808| With ID-ONLY as a non-nil value, produce links that consist only
01809| of the identifier, thus deviating from CURRENT-FILE-TYPE.
01810| 
01811| With optional REVERSE as a non-nil value, reverse the sort order.
01812| 
01813| With optional EXCLUDE-REGEXP exclude the files that match the given
01814| regular expression.  This is done after FILES-MATCHING-REGEXP and
01815| OMIT-CURRENT have been applied."
01816|   (denote-link--prepare-links
01817|    (denote-sort-get-directory-files files-matching-regexp sort-by-component reverse exclude-regexp)
01818|    current-file-type
01819|    id-only))

01862| (defun denote-sort-dired--prompts ()

01865|     (dolist (prompt denote-sort-dired-extra-prompts)
01866|       (pcase prompt
01867|         ('sort-by-component (setq sort-by-component (denote-sort-component-prompt)))
01868|         ('reverse-sort (setq reverse-sort (y-or-n-p "Reverse sort? ")))
01869|         ('exclude-regexp (setq exclude-rx (denote-sort-exclude-files-prompt)))))
01870|     (list sort-by-component reverse-sort exclude-rx)))

01880| EXCLUDE-REGEXP all have the same meaning as `denote-sort-dired'.

01889|    :special-buffer))

01891| (defun denote-sort-dired--get-sort-parameters (sort-by-component reverse)
01892|   "Return (SORT-BY-COMPONENT . REVERSE) for `denote-sort-dired'.
01893| If SORT-BY-COMPONENT is nil, use the value of the user option
01894| `denote-sort-dired-default-sort-component' or fall back to `identifier'.
01895| 
01896| If REVERSE is nil, use the value of the user option
01897| `denote-sort-dired-default-reverse-sort' or fall back to nil"
01898|   (cons
01899|    (or sort-by-component denote-sort-dired-default-sort-component 'identifier)
01900|    (or reverse denote-sort-dired-default-reverse-sort nil)))

01902| (defvar denote-dired-empty-mode-map
01903|   (let ((map (make-sparse-keymap)))
01904|     (define-key map (kbd "q") #'quit-window)
01905|     (define-key map (kbd "k") #'kill-buffer-and-window)
01906|     ;; TODO 2025-07-08: Maybe this is worth implementing.  The idea is
01907|     ;; to go back to the search.
01908|     ;;
01909|     ;; (define-key map (kbd "g") #'denote-dired-empty-revert-buffer)
01910|     map)
01911|   "Key map for `denote-dired-empty-mode'.")
01912| 
01913| (define-derived-mode denote-dired-empty-mode special-mode "Denote Dired Empty"
01914|   "Major mode of a `denote-sort-dired' that no longer matches anything."
01915|   :interactive nil
01916|   (let ((inhibit-read-only t))
01917|     (erase-buffer)
01918|     (delete-all-overlays)
01919|     (insert (propertize "Denote Dired" 'face 'bold)
01920|             "\n"
01921|             (make-separator-line)
01922|             "\n"
01923|             (propertize "No more matching files" 'face 'warning))))
01924| 
01925| (defun denote-sort-dired--prepare-buffer (directory files-fn buffer-name)
01926|   "Prepare buffer for `denote-sort-dired'.
01927| DIRECTORY is an absolute path to the `default-directory' of the Dired
01928| listing.
01929| 
01930| FILES-FN is a function that returns the files to be listed in the Dired
01931| buffer.
01932| 
01933| BUFFER-NAME is the name of the resulting buffer."
01934|   (let* ((default-directory directory)
01935|          (files (funcall files-fn))
01936|          (dired-buffer (dired (cons directory files))))
01937|     (with-current-buffer dired-buffer
01938|       (rename-buffer buffer-name :unique)
01939|       (setq-local revert-buffer-function
01940|                   (lambda (&rest _)
01941|                     (if-let* ((default-directory directory)
01942|                               (files (funcall files-fn)))
01943|                         (progn
01944|                           (setq-local dired-directory (cons directory files))
01945|                           (dired-revert))
01946|                       (denote-dired-empty-mode)))))
01947|     buffer-name))
01948| 
01949| ;;;###autoload
01950| (defun denote-sort-dired (files-matching-regexp sort-by-component reverse exclude-regexp)
01951|   "Produce Dired buffer with sorted files from variable `denote-directory'.
01952| When called interactively, prompt for FILES-MATCHING-REGEXP and,
01953| depending on the value of the user option `denote-sort-dired-extra-prompts',
01954| also prompt for SORT-BY-COMPONENT, REVERSE, and EXCLUDE-REGEXP.
01955| 
01956| 1. FILES-MATCHING-REGEXP limits the list of Denote files to
01957|    those matching the provided regular expression.
01958| 
01959| 2. SORT-BY-COMPONENT sorts the files by their file name component (one
01960|    among `denote-sort-components').  If it is nil, sorting is performed
01961|    according to the user option `denote-sort-dired-default-sort-component',
01962|    falling back to the identifier.
01963| 
01964| 3. REVERSE is a boolean to reverse the order when it is a non-nil value.
01965|    If `denote-sort-dired-extra-prompts' is configured to skip this
01966|    prompt, then the sorting is done according to the user option
01967|    `denote-sort-dired-default-reverse-sort', falling back to
01968|    nil (i.e. no reverse sort).
01969| 
01970| 4. EXCLUDE-REGEXP excludes the files that match the given regular
01971|    expression.  This is done after FILES-MATCHING-REGEXP and
01972|    OMIT-CURRENT have been applied.
01973| 
01974| When called from Lisp, the arguments are a string, a symbol among
01975| `denote-sort-components', a non-nil value, and a string, respectively."
01976|   (interactive (append (list (denote-files-matching-regexp-prompt)) (denote-sort-dired--prompts)))
01977|   (pcase-let* ((`(,component . ,reverse-sort) (denote-sort-dired--get-sort-parameters sort-by-component reverse))
01978|                (roots (denote-directories))
01979|                (single-dir-p (null (cdr roots)))
01980|                (files-fn `(lambda ()
01981|                             (let ((files (denote-sort-get-directory-files ,files-matching-regexp ',component ,reverse-sort nil ,exclude-regexp)))
01982|                               (if ,single-dir-p
01983|                                   (mapcar #'file-relative-name files)
01984|                                 files)))))
01985|     (if-let* ((directory (if single-dir-p ; see comment in `denote-file-prompt'
01986|                              (car roots)
01987|                            (denote-directories-get-common-root)))
01988|               (files (funcall files-fn))
01989|               (buffer-name (funcall denote-sort-dired-buffer-name-function files-matching-regexp sort-by-component reverse-sort exclude-regexp)))
01990|         (denote-sort-dired--prepare-buffer directory files-fn buffer-name)
01991|       (message "No matching files for: %s" files-matching-regexp))))

03821|   "Use the file extension to detect the file type of FILE.
03822| 
03823| If more than one file type correspond to this file extension, use the
03824| first file type for which the :title-key-regexp in `denote-file-types'

03864| (defun denote-rename-file-and-buffer (old-name new-name)

03887|       (with-current-buffer buffer
03888|         (set-visited-file-name new-name nil t)))))

03969| (defun denote--get-front-matter-components-order (content file-type)
03970|   "Return the components in the order they appear in CONTENT given FILE-TYPE.
03971| 
03972| Return a list containing the symbols `title', `signature', `keywords',
03973| `identifier' and `date' in the order that they appear in TEXT.  TEXT can
03974| be any string.  For example, it can be a front matter template or an
03975| entire file content."
03976|   (let ((components-with-line-numbers '()))
03977|     (with-temp-buffer
03978|       (insert content)
03979|       (goto-char (point-min))
03980|       (when (re-search-forward (denote--title-key-regexp file-type) nil t 1)
03981|         (push `(,(line-number-at-pos) . title) components-with-line-numbers))
03982|       (goto-char (point-min))
03983|       (when (re-search-forward (denote--keywords-key-regexp file-type) nil t 1)
03984|         (push `(,(line-number-at-pos) . keywords) components-with-line-numbers))
03985|       (goto-char (point-min))
03986|       (when (re-search-forward (denote--signature-key-regexp file-type) nil t 1)
03987|         (push `(,(line-number-at-pos) . signature) components-with-line-numbers))
03988|       (goto-char (point-min))
03989|       (when (re-search-forward (denote--date-key-regexp file-type) nil t 1)
03990|         (push `(,(line-number-at-pos) . date) components-with-line-numbers))
03991|       (goto-char (point-min))
03992|       (when (re-search-forward (denote--identifier-key-regexp file-type) nil t 1)
03993|         (push `(,(line-number-at-pos) . identifier) components-with-line-numbers)))
03994|     (mapcar #'cdr
03995|             (sort components-with-line-numbers (lambda (x y) (< (car x) (car y)))))))
03996| 
03997| (defun denote--file-has-front-matter-p (file file-type)
03998|   "Return non-nil if FILE has at least one front-matter line, given FILE-TYPE.
03999| 
04000| This is checked against its front matter definition.  If the front matter
04001| definition has no lines, this function returns non-nil."
04002|   (let* ((front-matter (denote--front-matter file-type))
04003|          (file-content (with-current-buffer (find-file-noselect file) (buffer-string)))
04004|          (components-in-template (denote--get-front-matter-components-order front-matter file-type))
04005|          (components-in-file (denote--get-front-matter-components-order file-content file-type)))
04006|     (or (null components-in-template)
04007|         (seq-intersection components-in-template components-in-file))))

04009| (defun denote--get-front-matter-rewrite-prompt (final-components to-add to-remove to-modify old-and-new-front-matter-lines)
04010|   "Return the prompt for the front matter rewrite operation.
04011| 
04012| FINAL-COMPONENTS is the list of components to handle at the end of the
04013| rewrite operation.
04014| 
04015| TO-ADD, TO-REMOVE, and TO-MODIFY are the list of components that needs
04016| to be added, removed or modified.
04017| 
04018| OLD-AND-NEW-FRONT-MATTER-LINES is an alist containing the old and new
04019| front matter lines."
04020|   (let ((prompt "Replace front matter?"))
04021|     (dolist (component final-components)
04022|       (let ((old-line (alist-get 'old (alist-get component old-and-new-front-matter-lines)))
04023|             (new-line (alist-get 'new (alist-get component old-and-new-front-matter-lines)))
04024|             (next-prompt ""))
04025|         (cond ((memq component to-remove)
04026|                (setq next-prompt (format "\n-%s\n"
04027|                                          (propertize old-line 'face 'denote-faces-prompt-old-name))))
04028|               ((memq component to-add)
04029|                (setq next-prompt (format "\n-%s\n"
04030|                                          (propertize new-line 'face 'denote-faces-prompt-new-name))))
04031|               ((memq component to-modify)
04032|                (setq next-prompt (format "\n-%s\n-%s\n"
04033|                                          (propertize old-line 'face 'denote-faces-prompt-old-name)
04034|                                          (propertize new-line 'face 'denote-faces-prompt-new-name)))))
04035|         (setq prompt (concat prompt next-prompt))))
04036|     (concat prompt "?")))
04037| 
04038| (defun denote--get-final-components-for-rewrite (components-in-file components-in-template components-to-add)
04039|   "Return the final components to handle by a front matter rewrite operation.
04040| 
04041| COMPONENTS-TO-ADD is the list of components that have to be added to
04042| COMPONENTS-IN-FILE to build the list of components that will need to be
04043| handled during a front matter rewrite operation.
04044| 
04045| COMPONENTS-IN-TEMPLATE is the list of components in a front matter
04046| template.  They are used to determine how the COMPONENTS-TO-ADD are
04047| added to COMPONENTS-IN-FILE.
04048| 
04049| Example:
04050|           file = (title signature)
04051|       template = (title keywords date id signature)
04052| 
04053| The date line is missing from the file.  From the template, we find out
04054| that it needs to be added *after* a keywords line.  Since we don't have
04055| one in the file, we keep looking for a line to add it *after* and find a
04056| title line.  Had we not found the title line in the file, we would have
04057| searched for a line to insert it *before*.  We would have inserted the
04058| date line before the signature line, for example.
04059| 
04060| This is repeated until all missing components are added."
04061|   (let ((final-components (copy-sequence components-in-file)))
04062|     (dolist (component components-to-add)
04063|       (if-let* ((previous-components-in-template
04064|                  (seq-take-while (lambda (x) (not (eq x component))) components-in-template))
04065|                 (first-previous-component-in-file
04066|                  (seq-find (lambda (x) (memq x final-components)) (reverse previous-components-in-template))))
04067|           ;; Insert after the existing element.
04068|           (let ((sublist final-components))
04069|             (while sublist
04070|               (if (not (eq (car sublist) first-previous-component-in-file))
04071|                   (setq sublist (cdr sublist))
04072|                 (push component (cdr sublist))
04073|                 (setq sublist nil))))
04074|         (let* ((next-components-in-template
04075|                 (cdr (seq-drop-while (lambda (x) (not (eq x component))) components-in-template)))
04076|                (first-next-component-in-file
04077|                 (seq-find (lambda (x) (memq x final-components)) next-components-in-template)))
04078|           ;; Insert before the existing element.  The intention is to
04079|           ;; modify final-components, but it does not work when push
04080|           ;; is called on sublist on the first iteration of the loop.
04081|           (if (eq (car final-components) first-next-component-in-file)
04082|               (push component final-components)
04083|             (let ((sublist final-components))
04084|               (while sublist
04085|                 (if (not (eq (car sublist) first-next-component-in-file))
04086|                     (setq sublist (cdr sublist))
04087|                   (push component sublist)
04088|                   (setq sublist nil))))))))
04089|     final-components))
04090| 
04091| (defun denote-rewrite-front-matter (file title keywords signature date identifier file-type)
04092|   "Rewrite front matter of note after `denote-rename-file'.
04093| The FILE, TITLE, KEYWORDS, SIGNATURE, DATE, IDENTIFIER, and FILE-TYPE
04094| are given by the renaming command and are used to construct new front
04095| matter values if appropriate.
04096| 
04097| If `denote-rename-confirmations' contains `rewrite-front-matter',
04098| prompt to confirm the rewriting of the front matter."
04099|   (let* ((front-matter (denote--front-matter file-type))
04100|          (file-content (with-current-buffer (find-file-noselect file) (buffer-string)))
04101|          (components-in-template (denote--get-front-matter-components-order front-matter file-type))
04102|          (components-in-file (denote--get-front-matter-components-order file-content file-type))
04103|          (components-to-add '())
04104|          (components-to-remove '())
04105|          (components-to-modify '())
04106|          (new-front-matter (denote--format-front-matter title date keywords identifier signature file-type))
04107|          (old-and-new-front-matter-lines (denote--get-old-and-new-front-matter-lines file new-front-matter file-type)))
04108|     ;; Build the lists of components to add, remove, modify.
04109|     (dolist (component '(title keywords signature identifier date))
04110|       ;; Ignore the component if it is not in the template.  It is not added, removed or modified.
04111|       (when (memq component components-in-template)
04112|         (let ((value (pcase component ('title title) ('keywords keywords) ('signature signature) ('date date) ('identifier identifier))))
04113|           (cond ((and (not (memq component components-in-file))
04114|                       (denote--component-has-value-p component value))
04115|                  (push component components-to-add))
04116|                 ((and (memq component components-in-file)
04117|                       ;; The component can still be marked for modification.
04118|                       (not (memq component denote-front-matter-components-present-even-if-empty-value))
04119|                       (not (denote--component-has-value-p component value)))
04120|                  (push component components-to-remove))
04121|                 ((and (memq component components-in-file)
04122|                       (not (string= (alist-get 'old (alist-get component old-and-new-front-matter-lines))
04123|                                     (alist-get 'new (alist-get component old-and-new-front-matter-lines)))))
04124|                  (push component components-to-modify))))))
04125|     ;; There should be at least one component in the file and the template.
04126|     (when (and (seq-intersection components-in-file components-in-template)
04127|                (or components-to-add components-to-remove components-to-modify))
04128|       (when-let* ((final-components (denote--get-final-components-for-rewrite
04129|                                      components-in-file components-in-template components-to-add)))
04130|         (with-current-buffer (find-file-noselect file)
04131|           (when (or (not (memq 'rewrite-front-matter denote-rename-confirmations))
04132|                     (y-or-n-p (denote--get-front-matter-rewrite-prompt
04133|                                final-components
04134|                                components-to-add components-to-remove components-to-modify
04135|                                old-and-new-front-matter-lines)))
04136|             (save-excursion
04137|               (save-restriction
04138|                 (widen)
04139|                 (goto-char (point-min))
04140|                 ;; Position point at the beginning of the first front matter line
04141|                 (let ((first-component (car (seq-difference final-components components-to-add))))
04142|                   (re-search-forward
04143|                    (funcall (denote--get-component-key-regexp-function first-component) file-type) nil t 1)
04144|                   (goto-char (line-beginning-position)))
04145|                 ;; Do the modifications
04146|                 (dolist (component final-components)
04147|                   (let ((component-key-regexp-function (denote--get-component-key-regexp-function component))
04148|                         (new-line (alist-get 'new (alist-get component old-and-new-front-matter-lines))))
04149|                     (cond ((memq component components-to-remove)
04150|                            (re-search-forward (funcall component-key-regexp-function file-type) nil t 1)
04151|                            (delete-region (line-beginning-position) (line-beginning-position 2)))
04152|                           ((memq component components-to-add)
04153|                            (insert (concat new-line "\n")))
04154|                           ((memq component components-to-modify)
04155|                            (re-search-forward (funcall component-key-regexp-function file-type) nil t 1)
04156|                            (goto-char (line-beginning-position))
04157|                            (insert new-line)
04158|                            (delete-region (point) (line-end-position))
04159|                            (goto-char (line-beginning-position 2)))
04160|                           (t
04161|                            (goto-char (line-beginning-position 2))))))))))))))
04162| 
04163| ;;;;; The renaming commands and their prompts
04164| 
04165| (defun denote--rename-dired-file-or-current-file-or-prompt ()
04166|   "Return Dired file at point or the current file, else prompt for one.
04167| Throw error if FILE is not regular, else return FILE."
04168|   (or (dired-get-filename nil t)
04169|       buffer-file-name
04170|       (let* ((file (buffer-file-name))
04171|              (format (if file
04172|                          (format "Rename FILE Denote-style [%s]: " file)
04173|                        "Rename FILE Denote-style: "))
04174|              (selected-file (read-file-name format nil file t nil)))
04175|         (if (or (file-directory-p selected-file)
04176|                 (not (file-regular-p selected-file)))
04177|             (user-error "Only rename regular files")
04178|           selected-file))))
04179| 
04180| (defun denote-rename-file-prompt (old-name new-name)
04181|   "Prompt to rename file named OLD-NAME to NEW-NAME.
04182| Return non-nil if the file should be renamed.
04183| 
04184| If `denote-rename-confirmations' does not contain
04185| `modify-file-name', return t without prompting."
04186|   (or (not (memq 'modify-file-name denote-rename-confirmations))
04187|       (unless (string= (expand-file-name old-name) (expand-file-name new-name))
04188|         (y-or-n-p
04189|          (format "Rename %s to %s?"
04190|                  (propertize (file-name-nondirectory old-name) 'face 'denote-faces-prompt-old-name)
04191|                  (propertize (file-name-nondirectory new-name) 'face 'denote-faces-prompt-new-name))))))
04192| 
04193| (defun denote-add-front-matter-prompt (file)
04194|   "Prompt to add a front-matter to FILE.
04195| Return non-nil if a new front matter should be added.
04196| 
04197| If `denote-rename-confirmations' does not contain
04198| `add-front-matter', return t without prompting."
04199|   (or (not (memq 'add-front-matter denote-rename-confirmations))
04200|       (y-or-n-p
04201|        (format "Add new front matter to %s?"
04202|                (propertize (file-name-nondirectory file) 'face 'denote-faces-prompt-new-name)))))
04203| 
04204| ;; NOTE 2023-10-20: We do not need a user option for this, though it
04205| ;; can be useful to have it as a variable.
04206| (defvar denote-rename-max-mini-window-height 0.33
04207|   "How much to enlarge `max-mini-window-height' for renaming operations.")
04208| 
04209| (defun denote--generate-date-for-rename (file)
04210|   "Generate a date for FILE.
04211| 
04212| Respect `denote-generate-identifier-automatically'."
04213|   (if (or (eq denote-generate-identifier-automatically t)
04214|           (eq denote-generate-identifier-automatically 'on-rename))
04215|       (or (file-attribute-modification-time (file-attributes file))
04216|           (current-time))
04217|     nil))
04218| 
04219| (defvar denote-rename-rewrite-front-matter t
04220|   "When non-nil, rewrite the front matter if appropriate.
04221| The purpose of this variable is to be `let' bound to nil by a caller of
04222| the command `denote-rename-file' or related.  This will have the effect
04223| of not rewriting the file's front matter.")
04224| 
04225| (defun denote--rename-file (file title keywords signature date identifier)
04226|   "Rename FILE according to the other parameters.
04227| Parameters TITLE, KEYWORDS, SIGNATURE, DATE, and IDENTIFIER are as
04228| described in `denote-rename-file' and are assumed to be valid (TITLE and
04229| SIGNATURE are strings, KEYWORDS is a list, etc.).
04230| 
04231| This function only does the work necessary to rename a file
04232| according to its parameters.  In particular, it does not prompt
04233| for anything.  It is meant to be combined with
04234| `denote--rename-get-file-info-from-prompts-or-existing' to create
04235| a renaming command.
04236| 
04237| Respect `denote-rename-confirmations', `denote-save-buffers' and
04238| `denote-kill-buffers'."
04239|   (let* ((initial-state (if (find-buffer-visiting file) 'visited 'not-visited))
04240|          (file-type (denote-filetype-heuristics file))
04241|          (keywords (denote-keywords-sort keywords))
04242|          (directory (file-name-directory file))
04243|          (extension (denote-get-file-extension file))
04244|          (date (cond (date date)
04245|                      (denote-accept-nil-date date)
04246|                      (t (or (file-attribute-modification-time (file-attributes file))
04247|                             (current-time)))))
04248|          (old-identifier (or (denote-retrieve-filename-identifier file) ""))
04249|          ;; Handle empty id
04250|          (identifier (if (and (string-empty-p identifier)
04251|                               (or (eq denote-generate-identifier-automatically t)
04252|                                   (eq denote-generate-identifier-automatically 'on-rename)))
04253|                          (funcall denote-get-identifier-function
04254|                                   nil
04255|                                   (or date
04256|                                       (file-attribute-modification-time (file-attributes file))
04257|                                       (current-time)))
04258|                        identifier))
04259|          (identifier (cond ((string-empty-p identifier) identifier)
04260|                            ((string= old-identifier identifier) identifier)
04261|                            ((and (not (string-empty-p old-identifier)) (denote--file-has-backlinks-p file))
04262|                             (user-error "The identifier cannot be modified: that will break existing links"))
04263|                            (t (funcall denote-get-identifier-function identifier nil))))
04264|          (new-name (denote-format-file-name directory identifier keywords title extension signature))
04265|          (max-mini-window-height denote-rename-max-mini-window-height))
04266|     (when (and (file-regular-p new-name)
04267|                (not (string= (expand-file-name file) (expand-file-name new-name))))
04268|       (user-error "The destination file `%s' already exists" new-name))
04269|     ;; Modify file name, buffer name, or both
04270|     (when (denote-rename-file-prompt file new-name)
04271|       (denote-rename-file-and-buffer file new-name))
04272|     ;; Handle front matter if new-name is of a supported type (rewrite or add front matter)
04273|     (when (and denote-rename-rewrite-front-matter
04274|                (denote-file-has-supported-extension-p file)
04275|                (denote-file-is-writable-and-supported-p new-name))
04276|       (if (denote--file-has-front-matter-p new-name file-type)
04277|           (denote-rewrite-front-matter new-name title keywords signature date identifier file-type)
04278|         (when (denote-add-front-matter-prompt new-name)
04279|           (denote-prepend-front-matter new-name title keywords signature date identifier file-type))))
04280|     (when (and denote-used-identifiers (not (string-empty-p identifier)))
04281|       (puthash identifier t denote-used-identifiers))
04282|     (denote--handle-save-and-kill-buffer 'rename new-name initial-state)
04283|     (setq denote-current-data
04284|           (list
04285|            (cons 'title title)
04286|            (cons 'keywords keywords)
04287|            (cons 'signature signature)
04288|            (cons 'directory directory)
04289|            (cons 'date date)
04290|            (cons 'id identifier)
04291|            (cons 'file-type file-type)
04292|            (cons 'template "")))
04293|     (run-hooks 'denote-after-rename-file-hook)
04294|     new-name))
04295| 
04296| (defun denote--rename-get-file-info-from-prompts-or-existing (file)
04297|   "Retrieve existing info from FILE and prompt according to `denote-prompts'.
04298| 
04299| It is meant to be combined with `denote--rename-file' to create
04300| renaming commands."
04301|   (let* ((file-in-prompt (propertize (file-relative-name file) 'face 'denote-faces-prompt-current-name))
04302|          (file-type (denote-filetype-heuristics file))
04303|          (date (denote-retrieve-front-matter-date-value file file-type))
04304|          (identifier (or (denote-retrieve-filename-identifier file) ""))
04305|          (title (or (denote-retrieve-title-or-filename file file-type) ""))
04306|          (keywords (denote-extract-keywords-from-path file))
04307|          (signature (or (denote-retrieve-filename-signature file) "")))
04308|     (dolist (prompt denote-prompts)
04309|       (pcase prompt
04310|         ('title
04311|          (setq title (denote-title-prompt
04312|                       title
04313|                       (format "Rename `%s' with TITLE (empty to remove)" file-in-prompt))))
04314|         ('keywords
04315|          (setq keywords (denote-keywords-prompt
04316|                          (format "Rename `%s' with KEYWORDS (empty to remove)" file-in-prompt)
04317|                          (string-join keywords ","))))
04318|         ('signature
04319|          (setq signature (denote-signature-prompt
04320|                           signature
04321|                           (format "Rename `%s' with SIGNATURE (empty to remove)" file-in-prompt))))
04322|         ('identifier
04323|          (setq identifier (denote-identifier-prompt
04324|                            identifier
04325|                            (format "Rename `%s' with IDENTIFIER (empty to remove)" file-in-prompt))))
04326|         ('date
04327|          (setq date (denote-valid-date-p (denote-date-prompt
04328|                                           date
04329|                                           (format "Rename `%s' with DATE" file-in-prompt)))))))
04330|     (list title keywords signature date identifier)))
04331| 
04332| ;;;###autoload
04333| (defun denote-rename-file (file title keywords signature date identifier)
04334|   "Rename file and update existing front matter if appropriate.
04335| 
04336| Always rename the file where it is located in the file system:
04337| never move it to another directory.
04338| 
04339| If in Dired, consider FILE to be the one at point, else the
04340| current file, else prompt with minibuffer completion for one.
04341| When called from Lisp, FILE is a file system path represented as
04342| a string.
04343| 
04344| If FILE has a Denote-compliant identifier, retain it while
04345| updating components of the file name referenced by the user
04346| option `denote-prompts'.  By default, these are the TITLE and
04347| KEYWORDS.  The SIGNATURE is another one.  When called from Lisp,
04348| TITLE and SIGNATURE are strings, while KEYWORDS is a list of
04349| strings.
04350| 
04351| The IDENTIFIER is a string that has the format of variable
04352| `denote-date-identifier-format'.
04353| 
04354| If there is no identifier, create a new identifier using
04355| `denote-get-identifier-function'.  By default, it creates a new
04356| identifier using the date parameter, the date of last modification or
04357| the `current-time'.
04358| 
04359| In interactive use, and assuming `denote-prompts' includes a
04360| title entry, make the TITLE prompt have prefilled text in the
04361| minibuffer that consists of the current title of FILE.  The
04362| current title is either retrieved from the front matter (such as
04363| the #+title in Org) or from the file name.
04364| 
04365| Do the same for the SIGNATURE prompt, subject to `denote-prompts',
04366| by prefilling the minibuffer with the current signature of FILE,
04367| if any.
04368| 
04369| Same principle for the KEYWORDS prompt: convert the keywords in
04370| the file name into a comma-separated string and prefill the
04371| minibuffer with it (the KEYWORDS prompt accepts more than one
04372| keywords, each separated by a comma, else the `crm-separator').
04373| 
04374| For all prompts, interpret an empty input as an instruction to
04375| remove that file name component.  For example, if a TITLE prompt
04376| is available and FILE is 20240211T093531--some-title__keyword1.org
04377| then rename FILE to 20240211T093531__keyword1.org.
04378| 
04379| In interactive use, if there is no entry for a file name
04380| component in `denote-prompts', keep it as-is.
04381| 
04382| When called from Lisp, the special symbol `keep-current' can be
04383| used for the TITLE, KEYWORDS, SIGNATURE, DATE, and IDENTIFIER
04384| parameters to keep them as-is.
04385| 
04386| [ NOTE: Please check with your minibuffer user interface how to
04387|   provide an empty input.  The Emacs default setup accepts the
04388|   empty minibuffer contents as they are, though popular packages
04389|   like `vertico' use the first available completion candidate
04390|   instead.  For `vertico', the user must either move one up to
04391|   select the prompt and then type RET there with empty contents,
04392|   or use the command `vertico-exit-input' with empty contents.
04393|   That Vertico command is bound to M-RET as of this writing on
04394|   2024-02-13 08:08 +0200. ]
04395| 
04396| As a final step, ask for confirmation, showing the difference
04397| between old and new file names.  Do not ask for confirmation if
04398| the user option `denote-rename-confirmations' does not contain
04399| the symbol `modify-file-name'.
04400| 
04401| If FILE has front matter for TITLE and KEYWORDS, ask to rewrite
04402| their values in order to reflect the new input, unless
04403| `denote-rename-confirmations' lacks `rewrite-front-matter'.  When
04404| the `denote-save-buffers' is nil (the default), do not save the
04405| underlying buffer, thus giving the user the option to
04406| double-check the result, such as by invoking the command
04407| `diff-buffer-with-file'.  The rewrite of the TITLE and KEYWORDS
04408| in the front matter should not affect the rest of the front
04409| matter.
04410| 
04411| If the file does not have front matter but is among the supported file
04412| types (per the user option `denote-file-type'), add front matter to the
04413| top of it and leave the buffer unsaved for further inspection.  Save the
04414| buffer if `denote-save-buffers' is non-nil.
04415| 
04416| When `denote-kill-buffers' is t or `on-rename', kill the buffer
04417| if it was not already being visited before the rename operation.
04418| 
04419| For the front matter of each file type, refer to the variables:
04420| 
04421| - `denote-org-front-matter'
04422| - `denote-text-front-matter'
04423| - `denote-toml-front-matter'
04424| - `denote-yaml-front-matter'
04425| 
04426| Construct the file name in accordance with the user option
04427| `denote-file-name-components-order'.
04428| 
04429| Run the `denote-after-rename-file-hook' after renaming FILE.
04430| 
04431| This command is intended to (i) rename Denote files, (ii) convert
04432| existing supported file types to Denote notes, and (ii) rename
04433| non-note files (e.g. PDF) that can benefit from Denote's
04434| file-naming scheme.
04435| 
04436| For a version of this command that works with multiple files
04437| one-by-one, use `denote-dired-rename-files'."
04438|   (interactive
04439|    (pcase-let* ((file (denote--rename-dired-file-or-current-file-or-prompt))
04440|                 (`(,title ,keywords ,signature ,date ,identifier)
04441|                  (denote--rename-get-file-info-from-prompts-or-existing file)))
04442|      (list file title keywords signature date identifier)))
04443|   (let* ((file-type (denote-filetype-heuristics file))
04444|          (title (if (eq title 'keep-current)
04445|                     (or (denote-retrieve-title-or-filename file file-type) "")
04446|                   title))
04447|          (keywords (if (eq keywords 'keep-current)
04448|                        (denote-extract-keywords-from-path file)
04449|                      keywords))
04450|          (signature (if (eq signature 'keep-current)
04451|                         (or (denote-retrieve-filename-signature file) "")
04452|                       signature))
04453|          (date (if (eq date 'keep-current)
04454|                    (denote-retrieve-filename-identifier file)
04455|                  date))
04456|          (identifier (if (eq identifier 'keep-current)
04457|                          (or (denote-retrieve-filename-identifier file) "")
04458|                        identifier))
04459|          ;; Make the data valid
04460|          (date (denote-valid-date-p date))
04461|          (new-name (denote--rename-file file title keywords signature date identifier)))
04462|     (denote-update-dired-buffers)
04463|     new-name))
04464| 
04465| (defun denote-rename-file-title ()
04466|   "Convenience command to change the title of a file.
04467| Like `denote-rename-file', but prompts only for the title.
04468| 
04469| Add or remove a title in one go.  Do this by prepopulating the
04470| minibuffer prompt with the existing title.  The user can then modify it
04471| accordingly.  An empty input means to remove the title altogether.
04472| 
04473| Please check the documentation of `denote-rename-file' with regard to
04474| how a completion User Interface may accept an empty input."
04475|   (declare (interactive-only t))
04476|   (interactive)
04477|   (let ((denote-prompts '(title)))
04478|     (call-interactively #'denote-rename-file)))
04479| 
04480| (defun denote-rename-file-keywords ()
04481|   "Convenience command to change the keywords of a file.
04482| Like `denote-rename-file', but prompts only for keywords.
04483| 
04484| Add or remove keywords in one go.  Do this by prepopulating the
04485| minibuffer prompt with the existing keywords.  The user can then insert
04486| the `crm-separator' (normally a comma), to write new keywords or edit
04487| what is in the prompt to rewrite them accordingly.  An empty input means
04488| to remove all keywords.
04489| 
04490| Please check the documentation of `denote-rename-file' with regard to
04491| how a completion User Interface may accept an empty input."
04492|   (declare (interactive-only t))
04493|   (interactive)
04494|   (let ((denote-prompts '(keywords)))
04495|     (call-interactively #'denote-rename-file)))
04496| 
04497| (defun denote-rename-file-date ()
04498|   "Convenience command to change the date of a file.
04499| Like `denote-rename-file', but prompts only for the date.
04500| 
04501| Modify a date in one go."
04502|   (declare (interactive-only t))
04503|   (interactive)
04504|   (let ((denote-prompts '(date)))
04505|     (call-interactively #'denote-rename-file)))
04506| 
04507| (defun denote-rename-file-identifier ()
04508|   "Convenience command to change the identifier of a file.
04509| Like `denote-rename-file', but prompts only for the identifier.
04510| 
04511| Modify an identifier in one go.  Do this by prepopulating the
04512| minibuffer prompt with the existing identifier.  The user can then modify
04513| it accordingly.  An empty input means to remove the identifier
04514| altogether.
04515| 
04516| An identifier that is already used in links cannot be modified,
04517| otherwise all links will break.
04518| 
04519| Please check the documentation of `denote-rename-file' with regard to
04520| how a completion User Interface may accept an empty input."
04521|   (declare (interactive-only t))
04522|   (interactive)
04523|   (let ((denote-prompts '(identifier)))
04524|     (call-interactively #'denote-rename-file)))
04525| 
04526| (define-obsolete-function-alias 'denote-keywords-add 'denote-rename-file-keywords "3.0.0")
04527| (define-obsolete-function-alias 'denote-rename-add-keywords 'denote-rename-file-keywords "3.0.0")
04528| (define-obsolete-function-alias 'denote-keywords-remove 'denote-rename-file-keywords "3.0.0")
04529| (define-obsolete-function-alias 'denote-rename-rename-keywords 'denote-rename-file-keywords "3.0.0")
04530| 
04531| (defun denote-rename-file-signature ()
04532|   "Convenience command to change the signature of a file.
04533| Like `denote-rename-file', but prompts only for the signature.
04534| 
04535| Add or remove a signature in one go.  Do this by prepopulating the
04536| minibuffer prompt with the existing signature.  The user can then modify
04537| it accordingly.  An empty input means to remove the signature
04538| altogether.
04539| 
04540| Please check the documentation of `denote-rename-file' with regard to
04541| how a completion User Interface may accept an empty input."
04542|   (declare (interactive-only t))
04543|   (interactive)
04544|   (let ((denote-prompts '(signature)))
04545|     (call-interactively #'denote-rename-file)))
04546| 
04547| (define-obsolete-function-alias 'denote-add-signature 'denote-rename-file-signature "3.0.0")
04548| (define-obsolete-function-alias 'denote-remove-signature 'denote-rename-file-signature "3.0.0")
04549| 
04550| ;;;###autoload
04551| (defun denote-dired-rename-files ()
04552|   "Rename Dired marked files same way as `denote-rename-file'.
04553| Rename each file in sequence, making all the relevant prompts.
04554| Unlike `denote-rename-file', do not prompt for confirmation of
04555| the changes made to the file: perform them outright (same as
04556| setting `denote-rename-confirmations' to a nil value)."
04557|   (declare (interactive-only t))
04558|   (interactive nil dired-mode)
04559|   (let ((denote-used-identifiers (denote--get-all-used-ids))
04560|         (denote-rename-confirmations nil))
04561|     (if-let* ((marks (dired-get-marked-files)))
04562|         (progn
04563|           (dolist (file marks)
04564|             (pcase-let ((`(,title ,keywords ,signature ,date ,identifier)
04565|                          (denote--rename-get-file-info-from-prompts-or-existing file)))
04566|               (denote--rename-file file title keywords signature date identifier)))
04567|           (denote-update-dired-buffers))
04568|       (user-error "No marked files; aborting"))))
04569| 
04570| (defalias 'denote-dired-rename-marked-files 'denote-dired-rename-files
04571|   "Alias for `denote-dired-rename-files'.")
04572| 
04573| (defun denote-keywords--combine (combination-type user-input-keywords keywords)
04574|   "COMBINATION-TYPE is either `:add', `:remove' or `:replace'.
04575| 
04576| USER-INPUT-KEYWORDS are new keywords collected from the end-user.
04577| KEYWORDS are the existing keywords for the underlying file.
04578| 
04579| This function is an internal implementation function."
04580|   (cond
04581|    ((eq combination-type :add)
04582|     (seq-union keywords user-input-keywords))
04583|    ((eq combination-type :replace)
04584|     user-input-keywords)
04585|    ((eq combination-type :remove)
04586|     (seq-difference keywords user-input-keywords))
04587|    (t
04588|     (error "Unknown operation in denote-keywords--combine: %s"
04589|            combination-type))))
04590| 
04591| (defun denote-dired-rename-marked-files--change-keywords (combination-type keywords-prompt)
04592|   "COMBINATION-TYPE is either `:add', `:remove' or `:replace'.
04593| 
04594| KEYWORDS-PROMPT is the prompt we show the end-user, when taking keywords
04595| as input.
04596| 
04597| This function is an internal implementation function."
04598|   (if-let* ((marks (dired-get-marked-files)))
04599|       (let ((denote-prompts '())
04600|             (denote-rename-confirmations nil)
04601|             (user-input-keywords (denote-keywords-prompt keywords-prompt))
04602|             (denote-used-identifiers (denote--get-all-used-ids)))
04603|         (dolist (file marks)
04604|           (pcase-let* ((`(,title ,keywords ,signature ,date ,identifier)
04605|                         (denote--rename-get-file-info-from-prompts-or-existing file))
04606|                        (new-keywords (denote-keywords-sort (denote-keywords--combine combination-type user-input-keywords keywords))))
04607|             (denote--rename-file file title new-keywords signature date identifier)))
04608|         (denote-update-dired-buffers))
04609|     (user-error "No marked files; aborting")))
04610| 
04611| ;;;###autoload
04612| (defun denote-dired-rename-marked-files-with-keywords ()
04613|   "Rename marked files in Dired to a Denote file name by writing keywords.
04614| 
04615| Specifically, do the following:
04616| 
04617| - retain the file's existing name and make it the TITLE field,
04618|   per Denote's file-naming scheme;
04619| 
04620| - sluggify the TITLE, according to our conventions (check the
04621|   user option `denote-file-name-slug-functions');
04622| 
04623| - prepend an identifier to the TITLE;
04624| 
04625| - preserve the file's extension, if any;
04626| 
04627| - prompt once for KEYWORDS and apply the user's input to the
04628|   corresponding field in the file name, rewriting any keywords
04629|   that may exist while removing keywords that do exist if
04630|   KEYWORDS is empty;
04631| 
04632| - add or rewrite existing front matter to the underlying file, if it is
04633|   recognized as a Denote note (per the user option `denote-file-type'),
04634|   such that it includes the new keywords.
04635| 
04636| Construct the file name in accordance with the user option
04637| `denote-file-name-components-order'.
04638| 
04639| Run the `denote-after-rename-file-hook' after renaming is done.
04640| 
04641| Also see the specialized commands to only add or remove keywords:
04642| 
04643| - `denote-dired-rename-marked-files-add-keywords'.
04644| - `denote-dired-rename-marked-files-remove-keywords'."
04645|   (declare (interactive-only t))
04646|   (interactive nil dired-mode)
04647|   (denote-dired-rename-marked-files--change-keywords
04648|    :replace "Rename marked files with KEYWORDS, overwriting existing (empty to ignore/remove)"))
04649| 
04650| ;;;###autoload
04651| (defun denote-dired-rename-marked-files-add-keywords ()
04652|   "Like `denote-dired-rename-marked-files-with-keywords' to only add keywords."
04653|   (declare (interactive-only t))
04654|   (interactive nil dired-mode)
04655|   (denote-dired-rename-marked-files--change-keywords
04656|    :add "Add KEYWORDS to marked files"))
04657| 
04658| ;;;###autoload
04659| (defun denote-dired-rename-marked-files-remove-keywords ()
04660|   "Like `denote-dired-rename-marked-files-with-keywords' to only remove keywords."
04661|   (declare (interactive-only t))
04662|   (interactive nil dired-mode)
04663|   (denote-dired-rename-marked-files--change-keywords
04664|    :remove "Remove KEYWORDS from marked files"))
04665| 
04666| ;;;###autoload
04667| (defun denote-rename-file-using-front-matter (file)
04668|   "Rename FILE using its front matter as input.
04669| When called interactively, FILE is the variable `buffer-file-name' or
04670| the Dired file at point, which is subsequently inspected for the
04671| requisite front matter.  It is thus implied that the FILE has a file
04672| type that is supported by Denote, per the user option `denote-file-type'.
04673| 
04674| The values of `denote-rename-confirmations',
04675| `denote-save-buffers' and `denote-kill-buffers' are respected.
04676| 
04677| Only the front matter lines that appear in the front matter template (as
04678| defined in `denote-file-types') will be handled.
04679| 
04680| To change the identifier (date) of the note with this command, the
04681| identifier line (if present) of the front matter must be modified.
04682| Modifying the date line has no effect.
04683| 
04684| While this command generally does not modify the front matter, there are
04685| exceptions.  The value of the `date' line will follow that of the
04686| `identifier' line.  If they are both in the front matter template and
04687| the `date' line is missing, it will be added again.  Similarly, if they
04688| are both in the front matter template and the `date' line is present and
04689| the `identifier' line has been removed, the `date' line will be removed
04690| as well.  Also, if the keywords are out of order and
04691| `denote-sort-keywords' is non-nil, they will be sorted.  There will be a
04692| prompt for this if `denote-rename-confirmations' contains
04693| `rewrite-front-matter'.
04694| 
04695| Construct the file name in accordance with the user option
04696| `denote-file-name-components-order'."
04697|   (interactive (list (or (dired-get-filename nil t) buffer-file-name)))
04698|   (unless (denote-file-is-writable-and-supported-p file)
04699|     (user-error "The file is not writable or does not have a supported file extension"))
04700|   (let ((file-type (denote-filetype-heuristics file)))
04701|     (unless (denote--file-has-front-matter-p file file-type)
04702|       (user-error "The file does not appear to have a front matter"))
04703|     (let* ((front-matter-template (denote--front-matter file-type))
04704|            (components-in-template (denote--get-front-matter-components-order front-matter-template file-type))
04705|            (title (if (memq 'title components-in-template)
04706|                       (or (denote-retrieve-front-matter-title-value file file-type) "")
04707|                     (or (denote-retrieve-filename-title file) "")))
04708|            (keywords (if (memq 'keywords components-in-template)
04709|                          (denote-retrieve-front-matter-keywords-value file file-type)
04710|                        (denote-retrieve-filename-keywords-as-list file)))
04711|            (signature (if (memq 'signature components-in-template)
04712|                           (or (denote-retrieve-front-matter-signature-value file file-type) "")
04713|                         (or (denote-retrieve-filename-signature file) "")))
04714|            (identifier (if (memq 'identifier components-in-template)
04715|                            (or (denote-retrieve-front-matter-identifier-value file file-type) "")
04716|                          (or (denote-retrieve-filename-identifier file) "")))
04717|            (date (when (memq 'date components-in-template)
04718|                    (when-let* ((date-value (denote-retrieve-front-matter-date-value file file-type)))
04719|                      (denote-valid-date-p date-value))))
04720|            (denote-accept-nil-date t))
04721|       (denote--rename-file file title keywords signature date identifier)
04722|       (denote-update-dired-buffers))))
04723| 
04724| ;;;###autoload
04725| (defun denote-dired-rename-marked-files-using-front-matter ()
04726|   "Call `denote-rename-file-using-front-matter' over the Dired marked files.
04727| Refer to the documentation of that command for the technicalities.
04728| 
04729| Marked files must count as notes for the purposes of Denote, which means
04730| that they at least have an identifier in their file name and use a
04731| supported file type, per the user option `denote-file-type'.  Files that
04732| do not meet this criterion are ignored because Denote cannot know if
04733| they have front matter and what that may be."
04734|   (interactive nil dired-mode)
04735|   (if-let* ((marks (seq-filter
04736|                     (lambda (m)
04737|                       (and (file-regular-p m)
04738|                            (denote-file-is-writable-and-supported-p m)
04739|                            (denote-file-has-identifier-p m)))
04740|                     (dired-get-marked-files))))
04741|       (let ((denote-used-identifiers (denote--get-all-used-ids)))
04742|         (dolist (file marks)
04743|           (denote-rename-file-using-front-matter file))
04744|         (denote-update-dired-buffers))
04745|     (user-error "No marked Denote files; aborting")))
04746| 
04747| ;;;;; Creation of front matter
04748| 
04749| (make-obsolete 'denote-add-front-matter nil "Use `denote-rename-file' or related. Starting with version 4.0.0.")
04750| 
04751| ;;;###autoload
04752| (defun denote-change-file-type-and-front-matter (file new-file-type)
04753|   "Change file type of FILE and add an appropriate front matter.
04754| 
04755| If in Dired, consider FILE to be the one at point, else the
04756| current file, else prompt with minibuffer completion for one.
04757| 
04758| Add a front matter in the format of the NEW-FILE-TYPE at the
04759| beginning of the file.
04760| 
04761| Retrieve the title of FILE from a line starting with a title
04762| field in its front matter, depending on the previous file
04763| type (e.g.  #+title for Org).  The same process applies for
04764| keywords.
04765| 
04766| As a final step, ask for confirmation, showing the difference
04767| between old and new file names.
04768| 
04769| Important note: No attempt is made to modify any other elements
04770| of the file.  This needs to be done manually.
04771| 
04772| Construct the file name in accordance with the user option
04773| `denote-file-name-components-order'."
04774|   (interactive
04775|    (list
04776|     (denote--rename-dired-file-or-current-file-or-prompt)
04777|     (denote--valid-file-type (or (denote-file-type-prompt) denote-file-type))))
04778|   (let* ((initial-state (if (find-buffer-visiting file) 'visited 'not-visited))
04779|          (dir (file-name-directory file))
04780|          (old-file-type (denote-filetype-heuristics file))
04781|          (id (or (denote-retrieve-filename-identifier file) ""))
04782|          (date (denote-retrieve-front-matter-date-value file old-file-type))
04783|          (title (or (denote-retrieve-title-or-filename file old-file-type) ""))
04784|          (keywords (denote-retrieve-front-matter-keywords-value file old-file-type))
04785|          (signature (or (denote-retrieve-filename-signature file) ""))
04786|          (new-extension (denote--file-extension new-file-type))
04787|          (new-name (denote-format-file-name dir id keywords title new-extension signature))
04788|          (max-mini-window-height denote-rename-max-mini-window-height))
04789|     (when (denote-rename-file-prompt file new-name)
04790|       (denote-rename-file-and-buffer file new-name)
04791|       (denote-update-dired-buffers)
04792|       (when (and (denote-file-is-writable-and-supported-p new-name)
04793|                  (denote-add-front-matter-prompt new-name))
04794|         (denote-prepend-front-matter new-name title keywords signature date id new-file-type)
04795|         (denote--handle-save-and-kill-buffer 'rename new-name initial-state)))))
04796|

04903| (defface denote-faces-time-delimiter '((t :inherit shadow))
04904|   "Face for the delimiter between date and time in Dired buffers."
04905|   :group 'denote-faces
04906|   :package-version '(denote . "2.1.0"))
04907| 
04908| ;; The following matchers must obey the doc of `font-lock-keywords':
04909| ;;   - Have one parameter, the limit of the search
04910| ;;   - Set match-data (and restore it on failure)
04911| ;;   - Move point after the match (or restore it on failure).
04912| ;;   - Return t on success and nil on failure. re-search-forward returns (point) on success. It may be better to do the same.
04913| 
04914| (defun denote-faces-dired-file-name-matcher (limit)
04915|   "Find the file name in a Dired line, not looking beyond LIMIT."
04916|   (let ((initial-match-data (match-data))
04917|         (initial-point (point))
04918|         (line-found nil))
04919|     ;; Find the next non empty line that contains a Dired file name
04920|     (while (and (not line-found)
04921|                 (re-search-forward "^.+$" limit t))
04922|       ;; dired-move-to-filename moves the point even if it returns nil
04923|       (let ((saved-point (point)))
04924|         (if (and (dired-move-to-filename)
04925|                  (save-match-data
04926|                    (denote-file-has-denoted-filename-p (buffer-substring (point) (line-end-position)))))
04927|             (setq line-found t)
04928|           (goto-char saved-point))))
04929|     (if line-found
04930|         (let ((beginning-point (point)))
04931|           (goto-char (match-end 0))
04932|           (set-match-data (list beginning-point (match-end 0)))
04933|           (point))
04934|       (goto-char initial-point)
04935|       (set-match-data initial-match-data)
04936|       nil)))
04937| 
04938| (defun denote-faces-directory-matcher (limit)
04939|   "Match the directory in a Dired line, not looking beyond LIMIT."
04940|   (let ((initial-match-data (match-data))
04941|         (initial-point (point)))
04942|     (if (re-search-forward "\\(?1:.*/\\)[^/]*$" limit t)
04943|         (progn
04944|           (goto-char (match-end 1))
04945|           (set-match-data (list (match-beginning 1) (match-end 1)))
04946|           (point))
04947|       (goto-char initial-point)
04948|       (set-match-data initial-match-data)
04949|       nil)))
04950| 
04951| (defun denote-faces-signature-matcher (limit)
04952|   "Match the signature in a Dired line, not looking beyond LIMIT."
04953|   (let ((initial-match-data (match-data))
04954|         (initial-point (point)))
04955|     (if (or (re-search-forward "==\\(?1:[^/]*?\\)\\(@@\\|--\\|__\\|==\\|\\.\\)[^/]*$" limit t)
04956|             (re-search-forward "==\\(?1:[^/]*\\)$" limit t))
04957|         (progn
04958|           (goto-char (match-end 1))
04959|           (set-match-data (list (match-beginning 1) (match-end 1)))
04960|           (point))
04961|       (goto-char initial-point)
04962|       (set-match-data initial-match-data)
04963|       nil)))
04964| 
04965| (defun denote-faces-identifier-matcher (limit)
04966|   "Match a general identifier in a Dired line, not looking beyond LIMIT."
04967|   (let ((initial-match-data (match-data))
04968|         (initial-point (point)))
04969|     (if (or (re-search-forward "@@\\(?1:[^/]*?\\)\\(@@\\|--\\|__\\|==\\|\\.\\)[^/]*$" limit t)
04970|             (re-search-forward "@@\\(?1:[^/]*\\)$" limit t))
04971|         (progn
04972|           (goto-char (match-end 1))
04973|           (set-match-data (list (match-beginning 1) (match-end 1)))
04974|           (point))
04975|       (goto-char initial-point)
04976|       (set-match-data initial-match-data)
04977|       nil)))
04978| 
04979| (defun denote-faces-title-matcher (limit)
04980|   "Match the title in a Dired line, not looking beyond LIMIT."
04981|   (let ((initial-match-data (match-data))
04982|         (initial-point (point)))
04983|     (if (or (re-search-forward "--\\(?1:[^/]*?\\)\\(@@\\|__\\|==\\|\\.\\)[^/]*$" limit t)
04984|             (re-search-forward "--\\(?1:[^/]*\\)$" limit t))
04985|         (progn
04986|           (goto-char (match-end 1))
04987|           (set-match-data (list (match-beginning 1) (match-end 1)))
04988|           (point))
04989|       (goto-char initial-point)
04990|       (set-match-data initial-match-data)
04991|       nil)))
04992|

04994|   "Match the keywords in a Dired line, not looking beyond LIMIT."
04995|   (let ((initial-match-data (match-data))
04996|         (initial-point (point)))
04997|     (if (or (re-search-forward "__\\(?1:[^/]*?\\)\\(@@\\|--\\|__\\|==\\|\\.\\)[^/]*$" limit t)
04998|             (re-search-forward "__\\(?1:[^/]*\\)$" limit t))
04999|         (progn
05000|           (goto-char (match-end 1))

05214| (defun denote-format-link (file description file-type id-only)
05215|   "Prepare link to FILE using DESCRIPTION.
05216| 
05217| FILE-TYPE and ID-ONLY are used to get the format of the link.
05218| See the `:link' property of `denote-file-types'."

05224|     ;; Org format because it is still a usable link with the help of
05225|     ;; the command `org-open-at-point-global'.

05227|      (denote--link-format 'org))
05228|     (t
05229|      (denote--link-format file-type)))

05231|    description))

05233| ;; NOTE 2025-11-23: The only reason I have &optional is because I want
05234| ;; it to be backward compatible.  We used to have a single FILE
05235| ;; parameter.
05236| (defun denote-link-description-with-signature-and-title (file &optional file-type)
05237|   "Return link description for FILE with FILE-TYPE.
05238| For backward compatibility, FILE-TYPE is an optional parameter.  If it
05239| is nil, then compute FILE-TYPE internally.
05240| 
05241| - If the region is active, use it as the description.
05242| 
05243| - If FILE has a signature, then format the description as a sequence of
05244|   the signature text and the title with two spaces between them.
05245| 
05246| - If FILE does not have a signature, then use its title as the
05247|   description.
05248| 
05249| - If none of the above works, return an empty string.
05250| 
05251| This function is useful as the value of the user option
05252| `denote-link-description-format' (which can optionally be bound to a
05253| function)."
05254|   (let* ((type (or file-type (denote-filetype-heuristics file)))
05255|          (signature (denote-retrieve-filename-signature file))
05256|          (title (denote-retrieve-title-or-filename file type))
05257|          (region-text (denote--get-active-region-content)))
05258|     (cond
05259|      (region-text region-text)
05260|      ((and signature title) (format "%s  %s" signature title))
05261|      (title (format "%s" title))
05262|      (signature (format "%s" signature))
05263|      (t ""))))

05269|               (end (region-end))

05271|               (_ (not (string-blank-p contents))))

05281| (defun denote-get-link-description (file &optional file-type)
05282|   "Return a link description for FILE.
05283| 
05284| If `denote-link-description-format' is a function, call it with FILE and
05285| FILE-TYPE as argument.  It should return a string, representing the link
05286| description.
05287| 
05288| If the user option `denote-link-description-format' is a string, parse
05289| it to substitute any format specifiers therein with their respective
05290| values (see the documentation of that user option).  If the region is
05291| active, use it as the description.
05292| 
05293| For backward compatibility, support the scenario where the function
05294| assigned to `denote-link-description-format' accepts a single FILE
05295| argument.  In that case, the function takes care to find the TYPE on its

05305|                 ;;
05306|                 ;;     (let ((errors nil))
05307|                 ;;       (mapatoms
05308|                 ;;        (lambda (symbol)
05309|                 ;;          (when (get symbol 'error-conditions)
05310|                 ;;            (push symbol errors))))
05311|                 ;;       errors)

05313|                 ;; As for `error-conditions', I looked into the source
05314|                 ;; of `define-error' to figure out what an "error" is
05315|                 ;; and saw the property there.
05316|                 (description (ignore-error wrong-number-of-arguments
05317|                                (funcall denote-link-description-format file file-type))))
05318|       description))
05319|    ((functionp denote-link-description-format)
05320|     (display-warning 'denote "The `denote-link-description-format' function is now called with FILE and FILE-TYPE" :warning)
05321|     (funcall denote-link-description-format file))

05330|                                       ((denote-retrieve-filename-title file))
05331|                                       (t  "")))
05332|                             (cons ?T (or (denote-retrieve-filename-title file) ""))
05333|                             (cons ?i (or (denote-retrieve-filename-identifier file) ""))

05361| ;;;###autoload
05362| (defun denote-link (file file-type description &optional id-only)
05363|   "Create link to FILE note in variable `denote-directory' with DESCRIPTION.
05364| 
05365| When called interactively, prompt for FILE using completion.  In this
05366| case, derive FILE-TYPE from the current buffer.  FILE-TYPE is used to
05367| determine the format of the link.
05368| 
05369| Return the DESCRIPTION of the link in the format specified by
05370| `denote-link-description-format'.  The default is to return the text of
05371| the active region or the title of the note (plus the signature if
05372| present).
05373| 
05374| With optional ID-ONLY as a non-nil argument, such as with a universal
05375| prefix (\\[universal-argument]), insert links with just the identifier
05376| and no further description.  In this case, the link format is always
05377| [[denote:IDENTIFIER]].

05379| If the DESCRIPTION is empty, format the link the same as with ID-ONLY.
05380| 
05381| When called from Lisp, FILE is a string representing a full file system
05382| path.  FILE-TYPE is a symbol as described in the user option
05383| `denote-file-type'.  DESCRIPTION is a string.  Whether the caller treats
05384| the active region specially, is up to it."
05385|   (interactive
05386|    (let* ((file (denote-file-prompt nil "Link to FILE" nil :has-identifier))
05387|           (file-type (denote-filetype-heuristics buffer-file-name))
05388|           (description (when (file-exists-p file)
05389|                          (denote-get-link-description file))))
05390|      (list file file-type description current-prefix-arg)))
05391|   (unless (or (denote--file-type-org-extra-p)
05392|               (and buffer-file-name (denote-file-has-supported-extension-p buffer-file-name)))
05393|     (user-error "The current file type is not recognized by Denote"))
05394|   (unless (file-exists-p file)
05395|     (user-error "The linked file does not exist"))
05396|   (denote--delete-active-region-content)
05397|   (insert (denote-format-link file description file-type id-only)))
