05460|   (when-let* ((current-file (or file (buffer-file-name)))
05461|               ((denote-file-has-supported-extension-p current-file))
05462|               (file-type (denote-filetype-heuristics current-file))
05463|               (regexp (denote--link-in-context-regexp file-type))
05464|               (files (or files (denote-directory-files nil nil nil nil :has-identifier)))
05465|               (file-identifiers
05466|                (with-temp-buffer
05467|                  (insert-file-contents current-file)
05468|                  (denote-link--collect-identifiers regexp)))
05469|               (file-identifiers-hash-table (make-hash-table :test #'equal)))
05470|     (dolist (id file-identifiers)
05471|       (puthash id t file-identifiers-hash-table))
05472|     (let ((found-files))
05473|       (dolist (file files)
05474|         (when (gethash (denote-retrieve-filename-identifier file) file-identifiers-hash-table)
05475|           (push file found-files)))
05476|       found-files)))
05477| 
05478| ;;;###autoload
05479| (defun denote-find-link ()
05480|   "Use minibuffer completion to visit linked file.
05481| Also see `denote-find-backlink'."
05482|   (declare (interactive-only t))
05483|   (interactive)
05484|   (when-let* ((links (or (denote-get-links)
05485|                          (user-error "No links found")))
05486|               (selected (denote-select-from-files-prompt links "Select among LINKS")))
05487|     (find-file selected)))
05488| 
05489| ;;;###autoload
05490| (defun denote-link-after-creating (&optional id-only)
05491|   "Create new note in the background and link to it directly.
05492| 
05493| Use `denote' interactively to produce the new note.  Its doc
05494| string explains which prompts will be used and under what
05495| conditions.
05496| 
05497| With optional ID-ONLY as a prefix argument create a link that
05498| consists of just the identifier.  Else try to also include the
05499| file's title.  This has the same meaning as in `denote-link'.
05500| 
05501| For a variant of this, see `denote-link-after-creating-with-command'.
05502| 
05503| IMPORTANT NOTE: Normally, `denote' does not save the buffer it
05504| produces for the new note.  This is a safety precaution to not
05505| write to disk unless the user wants it (e.g. the user may choose
05506| to kill the buffer, thus cancelling the creation of the note).
05507| However, for this command the creation of the note happens in the
05508| background and the user may miss the step of saving their buffer.
05509| We thus have to save the buffer in order to (i) establish valid
05510| links, and (ii) retrieve whatever front matter from the target
05511| file.  Though see `denote-save-buffer-after-creation'."
05512|   (interactive "P")
05513|   (unless (or (denote--file-type-org-extra-p)
05514|               (and buffer-file-name (denote-file-has-supported-extension-p buffer-file-name)))
05515|     (user-error "The current file type is not recognized by Denote"))
05516|   (let* ((type (denote-filetype-heuristics (buffer-file-name)))
05517|          (path (denote--command-with-features #'denote nil nil :save :in-background))
05518|          (description (denote-get-link-description path)))
05519|     (denote-link path type description id-only)))
05520| 
05521| ;;;###autoload
05522| (defun denote-link-after-creating-with-command (command &optional id-only)
05523|   "Like `denote-link-after-creating' but prompt for note-making COMMAND.
05524| Use this to, for example, call `denote-signature' so that the
05525| newly created note has a signature as part of its file name.
05526| 
05527| Optional ID-ONLY has the same meaning as in the command
05528| `denote-link-after-creating'."
05529|   (interactive
05530|    (list
05531|     (denote-command-prompt)
05532|     current-prefix-arg))
05533|   (unless (or (denote--file-type-org-extra-p)
05534|               (and buffer-file-name (denote-file-has-supported-extension-p buffer-file-name)))
05535|     (user-error "The current file type is not recognized by Denote"))
05536|   (let* ((type (denote-filetype-heuristics (buffer-file-name)))
05537|          (path (denote--command-with-features command nil nil :save :in-background))
05538|          (description (denote-get-link-description path)))
05539|     (denote-link path type description id-only)))
05540| 
05541| ;;;###autoload
05542| (defun denote-link-or-create (target &optional id-only)
05543|   "Use `denote-link' on TARGET file, creating it if necessary.
05544| 
05545| If TARGET file does not exist, call `denote-link-after-creating' which
05546| runs the `denote' command interactively to create the file.  The
05547| established link will then be targeting that new file.  In that case,
05548| use the last input at the file prompt as the default value of the title
05549| prompt.
05550| 
05551| With optional ID-ONLY as a prefix argument create a link that
05552| consists of just the identifier.  Else try to also include the
05553| file's title.  This has the same meaning as in `denote-link'."
05554|   (interactive
05555|    (let* ((target (denote-file-prompt nil "Select file (RET on no match to create it)" :no-require-match :has-identifier)))
05556|      (unless (and target (file-exists-p target))
05557|        (setq target (denote--command-with-features #'denote :use-file-prompt-as-def-title :ignore-region :save :in-background)))
05558|      (list target current-prefix-arg)))
05559|   (unless (or (denote--file-type-org-extra-p)
05560|               (and buffer-file-name (denote-file-has-supported-extension-p buffer-file-name)))
05561|     (user-error "The current file type is not recognized by Denote"))
05562|   (denote-link target
05563|                (denote-filetype-heuristics (buffer-file-name))
05564|                (denote-get-link-description target)
05565|                id-only))
05566| 
05567| (defalias 'denote-link-to-existing-or-new-note 'denote-link-or-create
05568|   "Alias for `denote-link-or-create' command.")

05628| (defgroup denote-query ()
05629|   "Integration between Denote and Xref for grep/query/backlink buffers."
05630|   :group 'denote)
05631| 
05632| (defcustom denote-query-sorting nil
05633|   "How to sort files in query buffers.
05634| This applies to buffers generated by the `denote-grep' command, query
05635| links for file contents, as well as backlinks.
05636| 
05637| By default (a nil value), no sorting of matching files is performed.
05638| Files are displayed in the order they are returned by the search
05639| program (which often, but not always, means they are sorted by file
05640| name).
05641| 
05642| The value can be a symbol among those listed in the value of the
05643| variable `denote-sort-components'.  Files will then be sorted according
05644| to the given file name component or the relevant method (e.g. randomly
05645| for the `random' symbol).
05646| 
05647| The value may also be a custom function.  It takes two arguments, as
05648| described by `sort' (internally, the function responsible is the
05649| `denote-sort-files').
05650| 
05651| Whatever the value of `denote-query-sorting', users may change the
05652| sorting of query buffers on demand by calling the command
05653| `denote-query-sort-last-search'."
05654|   :type '(radio
05655|           (const :tag "Don't sort (default)" nil)
05656|           (const :tag "Sort by identifier" identifier)
05657|           (const :tag "Sort by title" title)
05658|           (const :tag "Sort by keywords" keywords)
05659|           (const :tag "Sort by signature" signature)
05660|           (const :tag "Random order" random)
05661|           (const :tag "Last modified" last-modified)
05662|           (function :tag "Custom function that take two arguments for `sort'"))
05663|   :package-version '(denote . "4.1.0")
05664|   :group 'denote-query)
05665| 
05666| (defcustom denote-backlinks-display-buffer-action
05667|   '((display-buffer-reuse-mode-window display-buffer-below-selected)
05668|     (mode . denote-query-mode)
05669|     (dedicated . t)
05670|     (preserve-size . (t . t))
05671|     (window-height . fit-window-to-buffer)
05672|     (body-function . select-window))
05673|   "The action used to display the current file's backlinks buffer.
05674| 
05675| The value has the form (FUNCTION . ALIST), where FUNCTION is
05676| either an \"action function\", a list thereof, or possibly an
05677| empty list.  ALIST is a list of \"action alist\" which may be
05678| omitted (or be empty).
05679| 
05680| Sample configuration to display the buffer in a side window on
05681| the left of the Emacs frame:
05682| 
05683|     (setq denote-backlinks-display-buffer-action
05684|           (quote ((display-buffer-reuse-window display-buffer-in-side-window)
05685|                   (side . left)
05686|                   (slot . 99)
05687|                   (window-width . 0.3)
05688|                   (dedicated . t)
05689|                   (preserve-size . (t . t)))))
05690| 
05691| See Info node `(elisp) Displaying Buffers' for more details
05692| and/or the documentation string of `display-buffer'."
05693|   :risky t
05694|   :type `(choice
05695|           (alist :key-type
05696|                  (choice :tag "Condition"
05697|                          regexp
05698|                          (function :tag "Matcher function"))
05699|                  :value-type ,display-buffer--action-custom-type)
05700|           (function :tag "Custom function to return an action alist"))
05701|   :package-version '(denote . "4.2.0")
05702|   :group 'denote-query)
05703| 
05704| (defcustom denote-query-links-display-buffer-action
05705|   '((display-buffer-reuse-mode-window display-buffer-below-selected)
05706|     (mode . (denote-query-mode dired))
05707|     (dedicated . t)
05708|     (preserve-size . (t . t))
05709|     (window-height . fit-window-to-buffer)
05710|     (body-function . select-window))
05711|   "The action used to display query links.
05712| This is the same as `denote-backlinks-display-buffer-action'.  Refer to
05713| its documentation for the technicalities."
05714|   :risky t
05715|   :type `(choice
05716|           (alist :key-type
05717|                  (choice :tag "Condition"
05718|                          regexp
05719|                          (function :tag "Matcher function"))
05720|                  :value-type ,display-buffer--action-custom-type)
05721|           (function :tag "Custom function to return an action alist"))
05722|   :package-version '(denote . "4.2.0")
05723|   :group 'denote-query)
05724| 
05725| (defcustom denote-query-format-heading-function #'denote-get-file-name-relative-to-denote-directory
05726|   "Function used to construct headings for files matched by a query.
05727| 
05728| It is called with a single argument, the path to the note file, and it
05729| should always return a string.
05730| 
05731| This is used in the buffer that shows backlinks, query links for file
05732| contents, or the results of `denote-grep'."
05733|   :package-version '(denote . "4.2.0")
05734|   :link '(info-link "(denote) Use denote-grep to search inside files")
05735|   :group 'denote-query
05736|   :type 'function)
05737| 
05738| (defcustom denote-query-untitled-string "[Untitled]"
05739|   "String to use as heading for untitled notes in links' buffer.
05740| 
05741| Used only by `denote-query-extract-title'."
05742|   :package-version '(denote . "4.0.0")
05743|   :link '(info-link "(denote) Use denote-grep to search inside files")
05744|   :group 'denote-query
05745|   :type 'string)
05746| 
05747| (defun denote-query-extract-title (file)
05748|   "Extract note title from FILE front matter.
05749| 
05750| When no title is found, return title found in FILE name.
05751| 
05752| When that doesn't work, return `denote-grep-untitled-string'.
05753| 
05754| Intended to be used as `denote-query-format-heading-function'."
05755|   (if-let* ((type (denote-filetype-heuristics file))
05756|             (title (denote-retrieve-title-or-filename file type))
05757|             (_ (not (string-blank-p title))))
05758|       title
05759|     denote-query-untitled-string))
05760| 
05761| (defun denote--display-buffer-from-xref-alist (xref-alist buffer-name display-buffer-action)
05762|   "Create buffer called BUFFER-NAME for XREF-ALIST.
05763| 
05764| DISPLAY-BUFFER-ACTION is a `display-buffer' action and concomitant
05765| alist, such as `denote-backlinks-display-buffer-action'."
05766|   (let* ((inhibit-read-only t)
05767|          (file buffer-file-name)
05768|          (dirs (denote-directories)))
05769|     (unless xref-alist
05770|       (error "No results to display"))
05771|     ;; Update group of each item in xref-alist
05772|     (dolist (x xref-alist)
05773|       (let* ((file-xref (car x)))
05774|         (setf (car x) (funcall denote-query-format-heading-function file-xref))))
05775|     (with-current-buffer (get-buffer-create buffer-name)
05776|       (erase-buffer)
05777|       (denote-query-mode)
05778|       ;; In the links' buffer, the values of variables set in a
05779|       ;; `.dir-locals.el` do not apply.  We need to set
05780|       ;; `denote-directory' here because the buttons depend on it.
05781|       ;; Moreover, its value is overwritten after enabling the major
05782|       ;; mode, so it needs to be set after.
05783|       (setq-local denote-directory dirs)
05784|       (setq overlay-arrow-position nil)
05785|       (goto-char (point-min))
05786|       (xref--insert-xrefs xref-alist)
05787|       (goto-char (point-min))
05788|       (setq-local revert-buffer-function
05789|                   (lambda (_ignore-auto _noconfirm)
05790|                     (when-let* ((buffer-file-name file))
05791|                       (denote--display-buffer-from-xref-alist xref-alist buffer-name display-buffer-action)))))
05792|     (display-buffer buffer-name display-buffer-action)))
05793| 
05794| (defun denote-make-backlinks-buffer (identifier buffer-name display-buffer-action)
05795|   "Create links' buffer called BUFFER-NAME for IDENTIFIER.
05796| 
05797| DISPLAY-BUFFER-ACTION is a `display-buffer' action and concomitant
05798| alist, such as `denote-backlinks-display-buffer-action'."
05799|   (if-let* ((xref-alist (denote-retrieve-xref-alist-for-backlinks identifier)))
05800|       (denote--display-buffer-from-xref-alist xref-alist buffer-name display-buffer-action)
05801|     (error "No matches for identifier `%s'" identifier)))
05802| 
05803| ;; NOTE 2025-03-24: The `&rest' is there because we used to have an
05804| ;; extra SHOW-CONTEXT parameter.  This way we do not break anybody's
05805| ;; code, even if we slightly modify the behaviour.
05806| (defun denote-make-links-buffer (query &optional files buffer-name display-buffer-action &rest _)
05807|   "Create links' buffer called BUFFER-NAME for QUERY.
05808| 
05809| Optional FILES can be a list of files to search for.  It can also be a
05810| regexp, which limits the files accordingly per `denote-directory-files'.
05811| 
05812| Optional DISPLAY-BUFFER-ACTION is a `display-buffer' action and
05813| concomitant alist, such as `denote-backlinks-display-buffer-action'."
05814|   (if-let* ((inhibit-read-only t)
05815|             (buffer (or buffer-name
05816|                         (denote-format-buffer-name (format-message "query for `%s'" query) :special-buffer)))
05817|             (xref-alist (denote-retrieve-xref-alist query files))
05818|             (files (delete-dups (mapcar #'car xref-alist))))
05819|       (progn
05820|         (setq denote-query--last-query query)
05821|         (setq denote-query--last-files files)
05822|         (denote--display-buffer-from-xref-alist xref-alist buffer display-buffer-action))
05823|     (error "No matches for query `%s'" query)))
05824| 
05825| (defvar denote-query-links-buffer-function #'denote-make-links-buffer
05826|   "Function to make an Xref buffer showing query link results.
05827| It accepts the same arguments as `denote-make-links-buffer'.")
05828| 
05829| (defun denote--user-error-if-not-major-mode (mode)
05830|   "Signal `user-error' is MODE is not `derived-mode-p'."
05831|   (unless (derived-mode-p mode)
05832|     (user-error "Only use this command inside the `%s'" mode)))
05833| 
05834| (defun denote-query-focus-last-search (query)
05835|   "Search QUERY in the content of files which matched the last search.
05836| \"Last search\" here means any call to `denote-grep',
05837| `denote-backlinks', `denote-query-contents-link', or, generally, any
05838| command that relies on the `denote-make-links-buffer'."
05839|   (interactive
05840|    (or (denote--user-error-if-not-major-mode 'denote-query-mode)
05841|        (list (denote-grep-query-prompt "Search (only files matched last): ")))
05842|    denote-query-mode)
05843|   (denote--user-error-if-not-major-mode 'denote-query-mode)
05844|   (denote-make-links-buffer
05845|    query denote-query--last-files
05846|    nil '(display-buffer-same-window))
05847|   (message "Searching `%s' in files matched previously" query))
05848| 
05849| (defun denote-query-exclude-files (regexp)
05850|   "Exclude files whose name matches REGEXP from current search buffer.
05851| 
05852| This is useful even if you don't know regular expressions, given the
05853| Denote file-naming scheme.  For instance, to exclude notes with the
05854| keyword \"philosophy\" from current search buffer, type
05855| ‘\\<denote-query-mode-map>\\[denote-query-exclude-files] _philosophy
05856| RET’.
05857| 
05858| Internally, this works by generating a new call to
05859| `denote-make-links-buffer' with the same QUERY as the last one, but with
05860| a set of files gotten from checking REGEXP against last matched files.
05861| 
05862| When called from Lisp, REGEXP can be a list; in that case, it should be
05863| a list of fixed strings (NOT regexps) to check against last matched
05864| files.  Files that match any of the strings get excluded.  Internally,
05865| the list is processed using `regexp-opt'.  For an example of this usage,
05866| see `denote-query-exclude-files-with-keywords'."
05867|   (interactive
05868|    (or (denote--user-error-if-not-major-mode 'denote-query-mode)
05869|        (list (denote-grep-file-regexp-prompt)))
05870|    denote-query-mode)
05871|   (denote--user-error-if-not-major-mode 'denote-query-mode)
05872|   (let (final-files)
05873|     (dolist (file denote-query--last-files)
05874|       (unless (string-match
05875|                ;; Support list of strings as REGEXP
05876|                (if (listp regexp)
05877|                    (regexp-opt regexp)
05878|                  regexp)
05879|                file)
05880|         (push file final-files)))
05881|     (if final-files
05882|         (denote-make-links-buffer denote-query--last-query final-files
05883|                                   (and (eq major-mode 'denote-query-mode) (buffer-name))
05884|                                   '(display-buffer-same-window))
05885|       (user-error "No remaining files when applying that filter"))
05886|     (message "Excluding files matching `%s'" regexp)))
05887| 
05888| (defun denote-query-only-include-files (regexp)
05889|   "Exclude file names not matching REGEXP from current query buffer.
05890| 
05891| See `denote-query-exclude-files' for details, including the behaviour
05892| when REGEXP is a list."
05893|   (interactive
05894|    (or (denote--user-error-if-not-major-mode 'denote-query-mode)
05895|        (list (denote-grep-file-regexp-prompt :include)))
05896|    denote-query-mode)
05897|   (denote--user-error-if-not-major-mode 'denote-query-mode)
05898|   (let (final-files)
05899|     (dolist (file denote-query--last-files)
05900|       (when (string-match
05901|              ;; Support list of strings as REGEXP
05902|              (if (listp regexp)
05903|                  (regexp-opt regexp)
05904|                regexp)
05905|              file)
05906|         (push file final-files)))
05907|     (if final-files
05908|         (denote-make-links-buffer denote-query--last-query final-files
05909|                                   (and (eq major-mode 'denote-query-mode) (buffer-name))
05910|                                   '(display-buffer-same-window))
05911|       (user-error "No remaining files when applying that filter"))
05912|     (message "Only including files matching `%s'" regexp)))
05913| 
05914| (defun denote-query-exclude-files-with-keywords (keywords)
05915|   "Exclude files with KEYWORDS from current query buffer.
05916| 
05917| KEYWORDS should be a list of keywords (without underscore).
05918| 
05919| Interactively, KEYWORDS are read from the minibuffer using
05920| `completing-read-multiple', which see."
05921|   (interactive
05922|    (or (denote--user-error-if-not-major-mode 'denote-query-mode)
05923|        (list (denote-keywords-prompt "Exclude files with keywords")))
05924|    denote-query-mode)
05925|   (denote--user-error-if-not-major-mode 'denote-query-mode)
05926|   (denote-query-exclude-files
05927|    (mapcar (lambda (kw) (concat "_" kw)) keywords)))
05928| 
05929| (defun denote-query-only-include-files-with-keywords (keywords)

06329| ;; Adapted from `org-in-regexp'.
06330| (defun denote--inside-link-regexp-p (regexp position)
06331|   "Check if POSITION is inside a Denote link REGEXP.
06332| Return either nil or a list whose elements are two cons cells:
06333| 
06334| - The first cons cell has the link target and the link description,
06335|   like (\"denote:20250816T080008\" . \"This is a test\").
06336| 
06337| - The second cons cell consists of two buffer positions, pointing to the
06338|   beginning and end of REGEXP."
06339|   (catch 'exit
06340|     (let ((line-end (line-end-position)))
06341|       (save-excursion
06342|         (forward-line 0)
06343|         (while (and (re-search-forward regexp line-end t)
06344|                     (<= (match-beginning 0) position))
06345|           (when (>= (match-end 0) position)
06346|             (throw 'exit (list (cons
06347|                                 (match-string-no-properties 1)
06348|                                 (match-string-no-properties 2))
06349|                                (cons
06350|                                 (match-beginning 0)
06351|                                 (match-end 0))))))))))

06402|   "Set `denote-fontify-links--data'.
06403| Use optional DATA, else get the data with `denote-fontify-links--get-data'."
06404|   (setq-local denote-fontify-links--data (denote-fontify-links--get-data :force)))
06405| 
06406| ;; Implementation based on the function `org-activate-links'.
06407| (defun denote-fontify-links (limit)
06408|   "Provide font-lock matcher to fontify links up to LIMIT."
06409|   (pcase-let ((`(,type . ,query) (denote-fontify-links--get-data nil)))
06410|     (when (and type query)
06411|       (catch 'exit
06412|         (while (re-search-forward query limit t)
06413|           (let* ((start (match-beginning 0))
06414|                  (end (match-end 0))
06415|                  (visible-start (or (match-beginning 2) start))
06416|                  (visible-end (or (match-end 2) end))
06417|                  (query (match-string-no-properties 1)))
06418|             (let* ((properties `( mouse-face highlight
06419|                                   keymap ,denote-fontify-links-map
06420|                                   denote-link-query-part ,query
06421|                                   help-echo query
06422|                                   htmlize-link (:uri ,query)
06423|                                   font-lock-multiline t))
06424|                    (non-sticky-props
06425|                     '(rear-nonsticky (mouse-face highlight keymap invisible help-echo htmlize-link)))
06426|                    (face-property (denote-get-link-face query))
06427|                    (hidden (append '(invisible 'denote-fontified-link) properties)))
06428|               (remove-text-properties start end '(invisible nil))
06429|               (add-text-properties start visible-start hidden)
06430|               (add-face-text-property start end face-property)
06431|               (add-text-properties visible-start visible-end properties)
06432|               (add-text-properties visible-end end hidden)
06433|               (dolist (pos (list end visible-start visible-end))
06434|                 (add-text-properties (1- pos) pos non-sticky-props)))
06435|             (throw 'exit t)))
06436|         nil))))
06437| 
06438| (define-obsolete-function-alias
06439|   'denote-get-identifier-at-point
06440|   'denote-get-link-identifier-or-query-term-at-point
06441|   "4.0.0")
06442| 
06443| (defun denote-get-link-identifier-or-query-term-at-point (&optional position)
06444|   "Return the Denote identifier or query term at point or optional POSITION."
06445|   (let* ((data (denote--link-at-point-get-data (or position (point))))
06446|          (target (caar data)))
06447|     target))
06448| 
06449| (defun denote--get-link-file-path-at-point ()
06450|   "Return target file path of the Denote link at point.
06451| To be used as a `thing-at' provider."
06452|   (let* ((data (denote--link-at-point-get-data (point)))
06453|          (target (caar data)))
06454|     (when-let* ((path (denote-get-path-by-id target)))
06455|       (concat "file:" path))))
06456| 
06457| (defvar thing-at-point-provider-alist)
06458| 
06459| (define-obsolete-function-alias
06460|   'denote-fontify-links-mode-maybe
06461|   'denote-fontify-links-mode
06462|   "4.2.0")
06463| 
06464| ;;;###autoload
06465| (define-minor-mode denote-fontify-links-mode
06466|   "Fontify Denote links in plain text buffers.
06467| Do so only when the current buffer is a Denote note and the major mode
06468| is not `org-mode' or `markdown-mode' (or any major mode derived
06469| therefrom)."
06470|   :init-value nil
06471|   :global nil
06472|   :group 'denote
06473|   (require 'thingatpt)
06474|   (if (and buffer-file-name
06475|            (not (derived-mode-p 'org-mode 'markdown-mode))
06476|            (denote-file-is-in-denote-directory-p buffer-file-name)
06477|            (denote-file-has-supported-extension-p buffer-file-name)
06478|            (denote-file-has-denoted-filename-p buffer-file-name))
06479|       (progn
06480|         (if denote-fontify-links-mode
06481|             (progn
06482|               (add-to-invisibility-spec 'denote-fontified-link)
06483|               (denote-fontify-links--set-data)
06484|               (font-lock-add-keywords nil '((denote-fontify-links)))
06485|               (setq-local thing-at-point-provider-alist
06486|                           (append thing-at-point-provider-alist
06487|                                   '((url . denote--get-link-file-path-at-point)))))
06488|           (remove-from-invisibility-spec 'denote-fontified-link)
06489|           (kill-local-variable 'denote-fontify-links--data)
06490|           (font-lock-remove-keywords nil '((denote-fontify-links)))
06491|           (setq-local thing-at-point-provider-alist
06492|                       (delete
06493|                        '(url . denote--get-link-file-path-at-point)
06494|                        thing-at-point-provider-alist)))
06495|         (font-lock-update))
06496|     ;; NOTE 2026-01-02: If we do not set the value here, then it is
06497|     ;; toggled on/off even though the above `if' never reaches its
06498|     ;; THEN branch.
06499|     (setq denote-fontify-links-mode nil)
06500|     ;; NOTE 2026-01-02: In interactive use, we get a message that the
06501|     ;; mode is disabled if we call it in non-supported buffers.  I
06502|     ;; tried to `let' bind the `inhibit-message' but that did not
06503|     ;; work.  So I am doing this instead...
06504|     (when (called-interactively-p 'interactive)
06505|       (message "`denote-fontify-links-mode' works only in plain text buffers inside the `denote-directory'"))))
06506| 
06507| ;;;;; Add links matching regexp
06508| 
06509| (defvar denote-link--prepare-links-format "- %s\n"
06510|   "Format specifiers for `denote-add-links'.")
06511| 
06512| (defun denote-link--prepare-links (files current-file-type id-only &optional no-sort)
06513|   "Prepare links to FILES from CURRENT-FILE-TYPE.
06514| When ID-ONLY is non-nil, use a generic link format.
06515| 
06516| With optional NO-SORT do not try to sort the inserted lines.
06517| Otherwise sort lines while accounting for `denote-link-add-links-sort'."
06518|   (let ((links))
06519|     (dolist (file files)
06520|       (let* ((description (denote-get-link-description file))
06521|              (link (denote-format-link file description current-file-type id-only))
06522|              (link-as-list-item (format denote-link--prepare-links-format link)))
06523|         (push link-as-list-item links)))
06524|     (if no-sort
06525|         (nreverse links)
06526|       (sort links #'string-collate-lessp))))
06527| 
06528| (defun denote-link--insert-links (files current-file-type &optional id-only no-sort)
06529|   "Insert at point a typographic list of links matching FILES.
06530| 
06531| With CURRENT-FILE-TYPE as a symbol among those specified in variable
06532| `denote-file-type' (or the `car' of each element in `denote-file-types'),
06533| format the link accordingly.  With a nil or unknown non-nil value,
06534| default to the Org notation.
06535| 
06536| With ID-ONLY as a non-nil value, produce links that consist only
06537| of the identifier, thus deviating from CURRENT-FILE-TYPE.
06538| 
06539| Optional NO-SORT is passed to `denote-link--prepare-links'."
06540|   (when-let* ((links (denote-link--prepare-links files current-file-type id-only no-sort)))
06541|     (dolist (link links)
06542|       (insert link))))
06543| 
06544| ;;;###autoload
06545| (defun denote-add-links (regexp &optional id-only)
06546|   "Insert links to all files whose file name matches REGEXP.
06547| Use this command to reference multiple files at once.  Particularly
06548| useful for the creation of metanotes (read the manual for more on the
06549| matter).
06550| 
06551| Optional ID-ONLY has the same meaning as in `denote-link': it
06552| inserts links with just the identifier.
06553| 
06554| Also see `denote-link-to-all-files-with-contents'."
06555|   (interactive
06556|    (list
06557|     (denote-files-matching-regexp-prompt "Insert links to files matching REGEXP")
06558|     current-prefix-arg))
06559|   (unless (or (denote--file-type-org-extra-p)
06560|               (and buffer-file-name (denote-file-has-supported-extension-p buffer-file-name)))
06561|     (user-error "The current file type is not recognized by Denote"))
06562|   (let ((file-type (denote-filetype-heuristics (buffer-file-name))))
06563|     (if-let* ((files (denote-directory-files regexp :omit-current nil nil :has-identifier)))
06564|         (denote-link--insert-links files file-type id-only)
06565|       (message "No links matching `%s'" regexp))))
06566| 
06567| (defalias 'denote-link-to-all-files-with-regexp 'denote-add-links
06568|   "Alias for `denote-add-links'.")
06569| 
06570| ;;;;; Link to file with matching contents
06571| 
06572| ;;;###autoload
06573| (defun denote-link-to-file-with-contents (query &optional id-only)
06574|   "Link to a file whose contents match QUERY.
06575| This is similar to `denote-link', except that the file prompt is limited
06576| to files matching QUERY.  Optional ID-ONLY has the same meaning as in
06577| `denote-link'."
06578|   (interactive
06579|    (list (denote-query-link-prompt nil "Files whose contents include QUERY")))
06580|   (if-let* ((files (denote-retrieve-files-xref-query query))
06581|             ;; NOTE 2025-03-29: Maybe we should have a named prompt
06582|             ;; for this case, but I think we do not need it right now.
06583|             (file (completing-read
06584|                    (format "Select FILE with contents `%s': "
06585|                            (propertize query 'face 'denote-faces-prompt-current-name))
06586|                    (denote-get-completion-table files '(category . file))
06587|                    nil t nil 'denote-file-history)))
06588|       (denote-link file
06589|                    (denote-filetype-heuristics buffer-file-name)
06590|                    (denote-get-link-description file)
06591|                    id-only)
06592|     (user-error "No files include the query `%s' in their contents" query)))
06593| 
06594| ;;;###autoload
06595| (defun denote-link-to-all-files-with-contents (query &optional id-only)
06596|   "Link to all files whose contents match QUERY.
06597| This is similar to `denote-add-links', except it searches inside file
06598| contents, not file names.  Optional ID-ONLY has the same meaning as in
06599| `denote-link' and `denote-add-links'."
06600|   (interactive
06601|    (list (denote-query-link-prompt nil "Files whose contents include QUERY")))
06602|   (if-let* ((files (denote-retrieve-files-xref-query query)))
06603|       (denote-link--insert-links files (denote-filetype-heuristics buffer-file-name) id-only)
06604|     (user-error "No files include the query `%s' in their contents" query)))
06605|

06608| ;; TODO 2025-04-29: Rewrite the denote-link--buffer-file-prompt to be more general.
06609| ;; TODO 2025-04-29: Rewrite `denote-link-dired-marked-notes' to be more easy to reason about.
06610| 
06611| ;; NOTE 2022-07-21: I don't think we need a history for this one.
06612| (defun denote-link--buffer-file-prompt (buffer-file-names)
06613|   "Select file from BUFFER-FILE-NAMES of Denote notes."
06614|   (let* ((roots (denote-directories))
06615|          (single-dir-p (null (cdr roots)))
06616|          (file-names (if single-dir-p
06617|                          (mapcar
06618|                           (lambda (file)
06619|                             (denote--get-file-name-relative-to-directories file roots))
06620|                           buffer-file-names)
06621|                        buffer-file-names))
06622|          (selected (completing-read
06623|                     "Select open note to add links to: "
06624|                     (denote-get-completion-table file-names '(category . file))
06625|                     nil t)))
06626|     (if single-dir-p
06627|         (expand-file-name selected roots)
06628|       selected)))
06629| 
06630| (defun denote-link--map-over-notes ()
06631|   "Return list of `denote-file-has-denoted-filename-p' from Dired marked items."
06632|   (seq-filter
06633|    (lambda (file)
06634|      (and (denote-file-has-denoted-filename-p file)
06635|           (denote-file-has-identifier-p file)))
06636|    (dired-get-marked-files)))
06637| 
06638| ;;;###autoload
06639| (defun denote-link-dired-marked-notes (files buffer &optional id-only)
06640|   "Insert Dired marked FILES as links in BUFFER.
06641| 
06642| FILES conform with the Denote file-naming scheme, such that they can be
06643| linked to using the `denote:' link type.
06644| 
06645| The BUFFER is one which visits a Denote note file.  If there are
06646| multiple BUFFER candidates in buffers, prompt with completion for
06647| one among them.  If there is none, throw an error.
06648| 
06649| With optional ID-ONLY as a prefix argument, insert links with
06650| just the identifier (same principle as with `denote-link').
06651| 
06652| This command is meant to be used from a Dired buffer."
06653|   (interactive
06654|    (if (derived-mode-p 'dired-mode)
06655|        (list
06656|         (denote-link--map-over-notes)
06657|         (let ((file-names (denote--buffer-file-names)))
06658|           (find-buffer-visiting
06659|            (cond
06660|             ((null file-names)
06661|              (user-error "No buffers visiting Denote notes"))
06662|             ((eq (length file-names) 1)
06663|              (car file-names))
06664|             (t
06665|              (denote-link--buffer-file-prompt file-names)))))
06666|         current-prefix-arg)
06667|      (user-error "This command only works inside a Dired buffer"))
06668|    dired-mode)
06669|   (when (null files)
06670|     (user-error "No note files to link to"))
06671|   (unless (buffer-live-p buffer)
06672|     (error "The buffer `%s' is not live" buffer))
06673|   (let ((body (lambda ()
06674|                 (unless (or (denote--file-type-org-extra-p)
06675|                             (and buffer-file-name (denote-file-has-supported-extension-p buffer-file-name)))
06676|                   (user-error "The target file's type is not recognized by Denote"))
06677|                 (when (y-or-n-p (format "Create links at point in `%s'?" buffer))
06678|                   (denote-link--insert-links files (denote-filetype-heuristics buffer-file-name) id-only)
06679|                   (message "Added links to `%s'; displaying it now"
06680|                            ;; TODO 2024-12-26: Do we need our face here?  I think
06681|                            ;; not, but let me keep a note of it.
06682|                            (propertize (format "%s" buffer) 'face 'success))))))
06683|     (if-let* ((window (get-buffer-window buffer))
06684|               ((window-live-p window)))
06685|         (with-selected-window window (funcall body))
06686|       (with-current-buffer buffer (funcall body))
06687|       (display-buffer-below-selected buffer nil))))
06688| 
06689| (defalias 'denote-dired-link-marked-notes 'denote-link-dired-marked-notes
06690|   "Alias for `denote-link-dired-marked-notes' command.")
06691|

06814| (defun denote-context-menu (menu _click)
06815|   "Populate MENU with Denote commands at CLICK."
06816|   (define-key menu [denote-separator] menu-bar-separator)

06825| ;;;; Register `denote:' custom Org hyperlink
06826| 
06827| (declare-function org-link-open-as-file "ol" (path arg))
06828| 
06829| (defun denote-link--ol-resolve-link-to-target (link &optional full-data)
06830|   "Resolve LINK to target file, with or without additioanl file-search terms.
06831| With optional FULL-DATA return a list in the form of (path query file-search)."
06832|   (let* ((file-search (and (string-match "::\\(.*\\)\\'" link)
06833|                            (match-string 1 link)))
06834|          (query (if (and file-search (not (string-empty-p file-search)))
06835|                     (substring link 0 (match-beginning 0))
06836|                   link))
06837|          (path (denote-get-path-by-id query)))
06838|     (cond
06839|      (full-data
06840|       (list path query file-search))
06841|      ((and file-search (not (string-empty-p file-search)))
06842|       (concat path "::" file-search))
06843|      (t (or path query)))))
06844| 
06845| ;;;###autoload
06846| (defun denote-link-ol-follow (link)
06847|   "Find file of type `denote:' matching LINK.
06848| LINK is the identifier of the note, optionally followed by a file search
06849| option akin to that of standard Org `file:' link types.  Read Info
06850| node `(org) Query Options'.
06851| 
06852| If LINK is not an identifier, then it is not pointing to a file but to a
06853| query of file contents or file names (see the commands
06854| `denote-query-contents-link' and `denote-query-filenames-link').
06855| 
06856| Uses the function `denote-directory' to establish the path to the file."
06857|   (if-let* ((match (denote-link--ol-resolve-link-to-target link))
06858|             (_ (file-exists-p (string-trim-right match "::.*"))))
06859|       (org-link-open-as-file match nil)
06860|     (denote--act-on-query-link match)))

06943| ;;;###autoload
06944| (defun denote-link-ol-export (link description format)
06945|   "Export a `denote:' link from Org files.
06946| The LINK, DESCRIPTION, and FORMAT are handled by the export
06947| backend."
06948|   (pcase-let* ((`(,path ,query ,file-search) (denote-link--ol-resolve-link-to-target link :full-data))
06949|                (desc (cond
06950|                       (description)
06951|                       (file-search (format "denote:%s::%s" query file-search))
06952|                       (t (concat "denote:" query)))))
06953|     (if path
06954|         (pcase format
06955|           ('html (format "<a href=\"%1$s%3$s\">%2$s</a>" (denote-link--ol-export-get-relative-html path) desc (or file-search "")))
06956|           ('latex (format "\\href{%s}{%s}" (replace-regexp-in-string "[\\{}$%&_#~^]" "\\\\\\&" path) desc))
06957|           ('texinfo (format "@uref{%s,%s}" path desc))
06958|           ('ascii (format "[%s] <denote:%s>" desc path))
06959|           ('md (format "[%s](%s)" desc path))
06960|           (_ path))
06961|       (format-message "[[Denote query for `%s']]" query))))

07013| ;;;###autoload
07014| (defun denote-org-capture ()
07015|   "Create new note through `org-capture-templates'.
07016| Use this as a function that returns the path to the new file.
07017| The file is populated with Denote's front matter.  It can then be
07018| expanded with the usual specifiers or strings that
07019| `org-capture-templates' supports.
07020| 
07021| This function obeys `denote-prompts', but it ignores `file-type',
07022| if present: it always sets the Org file extension for the created
07023| note to ensure that the capture process works as intended,
07024| especially for the desired output of the
07025| `denote-org-capture-specifiers' (which can include arbitrary
07026| text).
07027| 
07028| Consult the manual for template samples."
07029|   (pcase-let* ((denote-prompts (remove 'file-type denote-prompts)) ; Do not prompt for file-type. We use org.
07030|                (`(,title ,keywords _ ,directory ,date ,identifier ,template ,signature)
07031|                 (denote--creation-get-note-data-from-prompts))
07032|                (`(,title ,keywords _ ,directory ,date ,identifier ,template ,signature)
07033|                 (denote--creation-prepare-note-data title keywords 'org directory date identifier template signature))
07034|                (front-matter (denote--format-front-matter title date keywords identifier signature 'org))
07035|                (template-string (cond ((stringp template) template)
07036|                                       ((functionp template) (funcall template))
07037|                                       (t (user-error "Invalid template")))))
07038|     (setq denote-last-path
07039|           (denote-format-file-name directory identifier keywords title ".org" signature))
07040|     (when (file-regular-p denote-last-path)
07041|       (user-error "A file named `%s' already exists" denote-last-path))
07042|     (denote--keywords-add-to-history keywords)
07043|     (concat front-matter template-string denote-org-capture-specifiers)))
07044|

07046| ;; by passing a single PROMPTS that is the same value as `denote-prompts'?

07048| ;;;###autoload
07049| (defun denote-org-capture-with-prompts (&optional title keywords subdirectory date template signature)
07050|   "Like `denote-org-capture' but with optional prompt parameters.
07051| 
07052| When called without arguments, do not prompt for anything.  Just
07053| return the front matter with title and keyword fields empty and
07054| the date and identifier fields specified.  Also make the file
07055| name consist of only the identifier plus the Org file name
07056| extension.
07057| 
07058| Otherwise produce a minibuffer prompt for every non-nil value that
07059| corresponds to the TITLE, KEYWORDS, SUBDIRECTORY, DATE, TEMPLATE,
07060| SIGNATURE arguments.  The prompts are those used by the standard
07061| `denote' command and all of its utility commands.
07062| 
07063| When returning the contents that fill in the Org capture
07064| template, the sequence is as follows: front matter, TEMPLATE, and
07065| then the value of the user option `denote-org-capture-specifiers'.
07066| 
07067| Important note: in the case of SUBDIRECTORY actual subdirectories
07068| must exist---Denote does not create them.  Same principle for
07069| TEMPLATE as templates must exist and are specified in the user
07070| option `denote-templates'."
07071|   (let ((denote-prompts '()))
07072|     (when signature (push 'signature denote-prompts))
07073|     (when template (push 'template denote-prompts))
07074|     (when date (push 'date denote-prompts))
07075|     (when subdirectory (push 'subdirectory denote-prompts))
07076|     (when keywords (push 'keywords denote-prompts))
07077|     (when title (push 'title denote-prompts))
07078|     (denote-org-capture)))

07088| ;;;; The `denote-rename-buffer-mode'
07089| 
07090| (defgroup denote-rename-buffer nil
07091|   "Rename Denote buffers to be shorter and easier to read."
07092|   :group 'denote
07093|   :link '(info-link "(denote) Top")
07094|   :link '(url-link :tag "Homepage" "https://protesilaos.com/emacs/denote"))
07095| 
07096| (defvaralias 'denote-buffer-has-backlinks-string 'denote-rename-buffer-backlinks-indicator
07097|   "Alias for `denote-rename-buffer-backlinks-indicator'.")
07098| 
07099| (defcustom denote-rename-buffer-backlinks-indicator " <-->"
07100|   "A string used to indicate that a buffer has backlinks pointing to it."
07101|   :type 'string
07102|   :package-version '(denote . "3.1.0")
07103|   :group 'denote-rename-buffer)
07104| 
07105| (defcustom denote-rename-buffer-format "%D"
07106|   "The format of the buffer name `denote-rename-buffer' should use.
07107| This also covers the `denote-rename-buffer-mode'.  The resulting buffer
07108| name will also include the `denote-buffer-name-prefix'.
07109| 
07110| The value of this user option is a string that treats specially the
07111| following specifiers:
07112| 
07113| - The %t is the Denote TITLE in the front matter or the file name.
07114| - The %T is the Denote TITLE in the file name.
07115| - The %i is the Denote IDENTIFIER of the file.
07116| - The %I is the identifier converted to DAYNAME, DAYNUM MONTHNUM YEAR.
07117| - The %d is the same as %i (DATE mnemonic).
07118| - The %D is a \"do what I mean\" which behaves the same as %t and if
07119|   that returns nothing, it falls back to %I, then %i.
07120| - The %s is the Denote SIGNATURE of the file.
07121| - The %k is the Denote KEYWORDS of the file.
07122| - The %b inserts `denote-rename-buffer-backlinks-indicator'.
07123| - The %% is a literal percent sign.
07124| 
07125| In addition, the following flags are available for each of the specifiers:
07126| 
07127| - 0 :: Pad to the width, if given, with zeros instead of spaces.
07128| - - :: Pad to the width, if given, on the right instead of the left.
07129| - < :: Truncate to the width and precision, if given, on the left.
07130| - > :: Truncate to the width and precision, if given, on the right.
07131| - ^ :: Convert to upper case.
07132| - _ :: Convert to lower case.
07133| 
07134| When combined all together, the above are written thus:
07135| 
07136|     %<flags><width><precision>SPECIFIER-CHARACTER
07137| 
07138| Any other string it taken as-is."
07139|   :type 'string
07140|   :package-version '(denote . "4.0.0")
07141|   :group 'denote-rename-buffer)
07142| 
07143| (defcustom denote-rename-buffer-function #'denote-rename-buffer
07144|   "Symbol of function that is called to rename the Denote file buffer.
07145| The default `denote-rename-buffer' function uses the pattern
07146| described in `denote-rename-buffer-format'.
07147| 
07148| Users can set this variable to an arbitrary function that does
07149| something else.  The function is called without arguments from
07150| the `find-file-hook' and `denote-after-new-note-hook'.
07151| 
07152| A nil value for this variable means that the title of the Denote
07153| buffer will be used, if available."
07154|   :type '(choice
07155|           (const :tag "Rename using the `denote-rename-buffer-format'" denote-rename-buffer)
07156|           (function :tag "Use a custom renaming function"))
07157|   :package-version '(denote . "2.1.0")
07158|   :group 'denote-rename-buffer)
07159| 
07160| (defun denote-rename-buffer--format (buffer)
07161|   "Parse the BUFFER through the `denote-rename-buffer-format'."
07162|   (when-let* ((file (buffer-file-name buffer)))
07163|     (let ((type (denote-filetype-heuristics file))
07164|           (should-show-backlink-indicator (and ; only do search if format contains "%b"
07165|                                            (string-match-p "%b" denote-rename-buffer-format)
07166|                                            (denote--file-has-backlinks-p file))))
07167|       (string-trim
07168|        (format-spec denote-rename-buffer-format
07169|                     (list (cons ?t (cond
07170|                                     ((denote-retrieve-front-matter-title-value file type))
07171|                                     ((denote-retrieve-filename-title file))
07172|                                     (t  "")))
07173|                           (cons ?T (or (denote-retrieve-filename-title file) ""))
07174|                           (cons ?b (if should-show-backlink-indicator denote-rename-buffer-backlinks-indicator ""))
07175|                           (cons ?i (or (denote-retrieve-filename-identifier file) ""))
07176|                           ;; TODO 2025-04-03: Maybe we can have something like `denote-date-format' here,
07177|                           ;; but I think we are okay with a hardcoded value.
07178|                           (cons ?I (or (when-let* ((id (denote-retrieve-filename-identifier file))
07179|                                                    (_ (denote-date-identifier-p id)))
07180|                                          (format-time-string "%A, %e %B %Y" (date-to-time (denote-id-to-date id))))
07181|                                        ""))
07182|                           (cons ?d (or (denote-retrieve-filename-identifier file) ""))
07183|                           (cons ?D (cond
07184|                                     ((denote-retrieve-front-matter-title-value file type))
07185|                                     ((denote-retrieve-filename-title file))
07186|                                     ((when-let* ((id (denote-retrieve-filename-identifier file)))
07187|                                        (if (denote-date-identifier-p id)
07188|                                            (format-time-string "%A, %e %B %Y" (date-to-time (denote-id-to-date id)))
07189|                                          id)))
07190|                                     (t  "")))
07191|                           (cons ?s (or (denote-retrieve-filename-signature file) ""))
07192|                           (cons ?k (or (denote-retrieve-filename-keywords file) ""))
07193|                           (cons ?% "%"))
07194|                     'delete)))))
07195| 
07196| (defun denote-rename-buffer (&optional buffer)
07197|   "Rename current buffer or optional BUFFER with `denote-rename-buffer-format'.
07198| The symbol of this function is the default value of the user
07199| option `denote-rename-buffer-function' and is thus used by the
07200| `denote-rename-buffer-mode'."
07201|   (when-let* ((file (buffer-file-name buffer))
07202|               ((denote-file-has-identifier-p file))
07203|               (new-name (denote-rename-buffer--format (or buffer (current-buffer))))
07204|               ((not (string-blank-p new-name))))
07205|     (rename-buffer (denote-format-buffer-name new-name) :unique)))
07206| 
07207| (defun denote-rename-buffer--fallback (&optional buffer)
07208|   "Fallback to rename BUFFER or `current-buffer'.
07209| This is called if `denote-rename-buffer-rename-function' is nil."
07210|   (let ((denote-rename-buffer-format "%t"))
07211|     (denote-rename-buffer buffer)))
07212| 
07213| (defun denote-rename-buffer-rename-function-or-fallback ()
07214|   "Call `denote-rename-buffer-function' or its fallback to rename with title.
07215| Add this to `find-file-hook' and `denote-after-new-note-hook'."
07216|   (funcall (or denote-rename-buffer-function #'denote-rename-buffer--fallback)))
07217| 
07218| ;;;###autoload
07219| (define-minor-mode denote-rename-buffer-mode
07220|   "Automatically rename Denote buffers to be easier to read.
07221| A buffer is renamed upon visiting the underlying file.  This
07222| means that existing buffers are not renamed until they are
07223| visited again in a new buffer (files are visited with the command
07224| `find-file' or related)."
07225|   :global t
07226|   (if denote-rename-buffer-mode
07227|       (progn
07228|         (add-hook 'denote-after-new-note-hook #'denote-rename-buffer-rename-function-or-fallback)
07229|         (add-hook 'denote-after-rename-file-hook #'denote-rename-buffer-rename-function-or-fallback)
07230|         (add-hook 'find-file-hook #'denote-rename-buffer-rename-function-or-fallback))
07231|     (remove-hook 'denote-after-new-note-hook #'denote-rename-buffer-rename-function-or-fallback)
07232|     (remove-hook 'denote-after-rename-file-hook #'denote-rename-buffer-rename-function-or-fallback)
07233|     (remove-hook 'find-file-hook #'denote-rename-buffer-rename-function-or-fallback)))

-(defun denote-dired-rename-marked-files-with-keywords ()
-  "Rename marked files in Dired to a Denote file name by writing keywords.
-
-Specifically, do the following:
-
-- retain the file's existing name and make it the TITLE field,
-  per Denote's file-naming scheme;
-
-- sluggify TITLE, according to our conventions (check the
-  user option `denote-file-name-slug-functions');
-
-- prepend an identifier to the TITLE;
-
-- preserve the file's extension, if any;
-
-- prompt once for KEYWORDS and apply user's input to the
-  corresponding field in the file name, rewriting any keywords
-  that may exist while removing keywords that do exist if
-  KEYWORDS is empty;
-
-- add or rewrite existing front matter to the underlying file, if it is
-  recognized as a Denote note (per user option `denote-file-type'),
-  such that it includes new keywords.
-
-Construct the file name in accordance with user option
-`denote-file-name-components-order'.

-

-

-- `denote-dired-rename-marked-files-remove-keywords'."
